Conflict rows use `tertiaryContainer.copy(alpha = 0.5f)` background per ADR-014 §6 — distinct from the Phase 37 traffic-light diff palette. Bottom-bar "Apply and merge" button gated on `canApplyAndMerge`. testTags: `chartConflictResolutionScreen` root + `conflictRow_<layerId>_<x>_<y>` / `layerConflictRow_<layerId>` per row + `takeTheirsButton_*` / `keepMineButton_*` / `skipButton_*` per pick + `applyAndMergeButton`. **PullRequestDetailScreen merge wiring**: merge button on action bar flips from `enabled = false` (Phase 38.3 deferred) to actively enabled. Merge confirmation dialog confirm button now dispatches `ConfirmMerge` event (was `DismissMergeConfirmation` no-op). New `onResolveConflicts: (prId: String) -> Unit` screen prop wired through NavGraph to `navigate(ChartConflictResolution(prId))`. Snackbar consumer extended to handle `PrMerged` (success toast) + `NavigateToConflictResolution` (push the resolution screen). **iOS mirror** at `iosApp/iosApp/Screens/ChartConflictResolutionScreen.swift` uses the established `ScopedViewModel<ChartConflictResolutionViewModel, ChartConflictResolutionState>` holder pattern. SwiftUI `List` with `Section`s for layer + cell conflicts; `ForEach(report.conflicts, id: \.id)` consumes the new `id` derived property added on `CellConflict` / `LayerConflict`. Conflict rows use `Color(.systemPurple).opacity(0.45)` per code review LOW-1 fix (was 0.18 — too faint at standard display brightness, asymmetric vs. Compose's 50% alpha). `AnyButtonStyle` private struct type-erases `PrimitiveButtonStyle` so the picker button can switch between `.borderedProminent` (selected) and `.bordered` (unselected) at runtime — SwiftUI's button-style protocol has an opaque `Body` associated type that prevents direct ternary switching; the closure-capture approach is the established idiom (see `AnyTransition`, `AnyShapeStyle`). **PullRequestDetailScreen.swift updates**: merge button on action bar drops `.disabled(true)`; merge confirmation dialog confirm dispatches `ConfirmMerge`; navEvent collector handles `PrMerged` (overlay toast `message_pr_merged_successfully`) + `NavigateToConflictResolution` (`path.append(Route.chartConflictResolution(prId:))`). **NavGraph**: new `@Serializable data class ChartConflictResolution(val prId: String)` route + `composable<ChartConflictResolution>` block plumbing `onMerged = { navController.popBackStack() }` so the user lands on the now-merged PR detail screen with status flip echoed via Realtime. `AppRouter.swift` `Route.chartConflictResolution(prId:)` enum case + Hashable conformance + destinationView mapping. **Koin DI**: `RepositoryModule` registers the merge port as `single<PullRequestMergeOperations> { get<RemotePullRequestDataSource>() }` — exposes the data-layer adapter through the domain-layer interface. `UseCaseModule` registers `MergePullRequestUseCase` factory with `getOrNull<PullRequestMergeOperations>()` so local-only mode (no Supabase) surfaces a Validation error rather than NPE. `ViewModelModule` registers `ChartConflictResolutionViewModel` parametric factory + extends `PullRequestDetailViewModel` factory with the 3 new optional deps. **iOS bridge**: `KoinHelper.kt` adds `getChartConflictResolutionViewModel(prId)` accessor + `wrapChartConflictResolutionState` (StateFlow → FlowWrapper) + `wrapChartConflictResolutionNavEvents` (Flow → EventFlowWrapper). `ViewModelFactory.swift` adds `chartConflictResolutionViewModel(prId:)` typed accessor. **i18n** — 10 new keys across all 5 sources (335 total, +10 from 325 baseline; matches the ADR §6 budget exactly): `title_resolve_conflicts`, `label_conflict_summary` parametric ("%1$d conflicts to resolve" EN / "解決が必要なコンフリクト: %1$d 件" JA — JA reorders with the `件` counter suffix per natural Japanese reading), `label_conflict_layer`, `label_conflict_cell` parametric ("Cell (%1$d, %2$d)" / "セル (%1$d, %2$d)"), `action_take_theirs` / `action_keep_mine` / `action_skip_conflict` (picker buttons), `action_apply_and_merge` (bottom-bar primary action), `state_all_conflicts_resolved` (summary chip when every conflict has a pick), `message_pr_merged_successfully` (deferred from Phase 38.3 — finally surfaced now that the merge UX lands). iOS xcstrings parametric specifiers use `%1$d`/`%2$d` for ints. **Tests (+35 commonTest, 1131 → 1166 — ADR-014 §8 budget was +20; overshoots justified by the 3-way ConflictDetector algorithm needing comprehensive partition coverage)**: `ConflictDetectorTest` (14 tests) covers the full coverage matrix including identical-clean, only-theirs / only-mine, both-modify-different / both-modify-same / both-add-different, theirs-removes-mine-modifies, parametric symbol parameter edits, layer added / renamed-different / renamed-identical, polar coordinate parity, multi-layer mixed change partitioning. `MergePullRequestUseCaseTest` (13 tests) covers status-not-open / unauthenticated / not-target-owner / offline-only Validations, happy path with revision-id round-trip, all 5 RPC error message → UseCaseError mappings, fresh-revision-id-per-call idempotency, plus the HIGH-1 + HIGH-2 regression tests `applyResolutions auto-clean preserves target-side autoFromMine edits` and `applyResolutions SKIP on cell whose layer was auto-removed drops the cell`. `ChartConflictResolutionViewModelTest` (8 tests) covers loadInitial → ConflictDetector run, canApplyAndMerge gating on cell + layer conflicts, PickCell / PickLayer state mutation, ApplyAndMerge happy path emitting MergeApplied event, ApplyAndMerge failure path surfacing state.error, revision lookup miss leaving report null with error, ClearError. New private test fakes: `FakeMergeOps` + `RecordingMergeOps` (in-memory `PullRequestMergeOperations` with last-call recording + throw-on-next failure injection); `FakeRevisionRepoForResolution` (revision-id keyed map). Also added a non-suspend `seed(pattern)` helper to `FakePatternRepository` so test fixtures can populate without `runTest` boilerplate. Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 2 HIGH / 2 MEDIUM / 3 LOW first pass — all 7 fixed pre-commit; second pass APPROVED with 0 findings. **HIGH-1** (auto-clean merge path passed `theirs` directly to `MergePullRequestUseCase` instead of the resolved document — silently dropped any target-side `autoFromMine` edits when the target branch had diverged from the ancestor since the fork point) fixed by routing through `applyResolutions` with empty conflict-resolution maps; regression test `applyResolutions auto-clean preserves target-side autoFromMine edits` lands the verification. **HIGH-2** (SKIP cell resolution against a layer auto-removed by theirs would silently recreate an orphan cell bucket that the final `mergedLayers` build never sees, dropping the SKIP outcome silently — KEEP_MINE on the same coordinate suffers the same bug) fixed by `if (!layersById.containsKey(coord.layerId)) continue` guard at the top of the `conflictPicks` loop; regression test `applyResolutions SKIP on cell whose layer was auto-removed drops the cell` lands the verification. **MEDIUM-1** (`PullRequestMergeOperations` was placed in `domain.usecase` package but implemented by `RemotePullRequestDataSource` in `data.remote` — crosses the layer boundary; should be in `domain.repository` matching the `ChartRevisionRepository` / `StructuredChartRepository` ports-and-adapters precedent) fixed by moving the interface to a new `domain/repository/PullRequestMergeOperations.kt` file; updated 4 import sites (`MergePullRequestUseCase.kt`, `RemotePullRequestDataSource.kt`, `RepositoryModule.kt`, `UseCaseModule.kt`, plus the two test files). **MEDIUM-2** (`LayerConflictRow` rendered `conflict.layerId` as the user-visible label — UUID strings are meaningless to users; should resolve a human-readable name from `conflict.theirs?.name ?: mine?.name ?: ancestor?.name ?: layerId` since at least one of theirs/mine is non-null on a PropertyChanged conflict) fixed on both Compose and SwiftUI. **LOW-1** (iOS row alpha asymmetric — Compose used 50% on tertiaryContainer, iOS used 18% on systemPurple, perceptually too faint at standard display brightness) fixed by bumping iOS to 0.45 with explanatory inline comment naming the Compose parity rationale. **LOW-2** (iOS `AnyButtonStyle` PrimitiveButtonStyle wrapper) confirmed correct — SwiftUI's button-style protocol has an opaque associated type so the closure-capture approach is the established idiom matching `AnyTransition` / `AnyShapeStyle`. **LOW-3** (`onCleared` not implemented on `ChartConflictResolutionViewModel`) confirmed correct — the VM has no Realtime subscriptions, no Channel teardown needs (`viewModelScope` cancellation handles `_navEvents` automatically), nothing to clean up. **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1166 tests, +35 from 1131 baseline), `:shared:koverVerify`, `bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` (335 keys). iOS app builds via `xcodebuild -project iosApp.xcodeproj -scheme iosApp -destination 'generic/platform=iOS Simulator' -configuration Debug build` ✅. **Closes Phase 38**: with this slice the entire ADR-014 collaboration loop — append-only data spine (38.1) → read-only PR list (38.2) → PR detail with open / close / comment write paths (38.3) → merge + conflict resolution (38.4) — is end-to-end functional. The `chart_revisions.author_id != owner_id` invariant from ADR-013 §1 finally has its first non-trivial use; the SECURITY DEFINER RPC pattern joins `delete_own_account` (ADR-005) as the second cross-table atomic-write precedent; the 3-way diff helper sits one layer above the Phase 37 §5 algorithm so a future "preview merge" affordance reuses it. **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-014 §10**: three-pane canvas preview deferred (`DualCanvasPanel` extraction is meaningful refactor; row-based picker alone closes the merge loop), Maestro E2E deferred (linked-pattern + open-PR + chart-divergence fixture prerequisite adds significant Maestro setup, no clear value gain over the 35 commonTest), "ChartViewer overflow → Open PR" entry remains deferred (the data layer + use case are wired and ready; UI flow is its own slice, likely 38.4.1 if it lands ahead of Phase 39), required-approval gates / draft PR / threaded comments / markdown all post-v1, "merge-conflict re-resolution after source drift mid-resolution" surfaces the generic "Source tip drifted" error today (better UX is post-v1).

- **Phase 38.3**: Pull request detail surface + open / close / comment write paths (ADR-014 §6, §8) — third code slice of Phase 38 builds the user-visible read+write surface for a single PR on top of the 38.1 data spine and 38.2 list. Closes the no-op `onPullRequestClick` callback the 38.2 NavGraph left wired. **No merge yet** — Phase 38.4 owns merge + conflict resolution. **5 new use cases** under `shared/.../domain/usecase/`: `GetPullRequestUseCase` (suspend invoke + `observe(prId, ownerId, scope)` Flow that filters whichever owner-scoped Flow the caller indicates so a status flip landing through Realtime emits a fresh state without a manual refresh — `PullRequestObserveScope` enum with INCOMING / OUTGOING decides which side to subscribe to based on the user's role; ViewModel picks INCOMING when `currentUserId == targetOwnerId`, OUTGOING when `currentUserId == authorId`); `GetPullRequestCommentsUseCase` (suspend invoke + observe Flow over the local cache — KDoc explicitly documents that the Realtime cold-launch seed is owned by the new `PullRequestRepository.subscribeToCommentsChannel` which kicks a remote fetch under the same lock as the channel attach, so the observe Flow stays warm thereafter via the per-PR Realtime channel); `PostPullRequestCommentUseCase` (validates body length ≤ 5000 chars per migration 016 CHECK + ADR-014 §1 client-side, rejects blank-after-trim bodies, generates the row id + `createdAt = Clock.System.now()` locally, calls repo `postComment`); `OpenPullRequestUseCase` (computes `commonAncestorRevisionId` client-side per ADR-014 §3 by snapshotting target's full history into a `Set<revisionId>` then walking source's `parent_revision_id` chain starting from `sourceTipRevisionId` until it hits a revision in the target set — the start revision itself counts so a fork-with-no-source-side-edits resolves the source tip immediately as the common ancestor; defense-in-depth `MAX_WALK_DEPTH = 1000` guards against pathological circular chains; `MAX_TARGET_HISTORY_LIMIT = 1000` covers any realistic per-pattern revision count without surfacing a pagination boundary; title ≤ 200 / description ≤ 2000 char validation per ADR-014 §1; if no ancestor found surfaces `UseCaseError.Validation` rather than writing a malformed PR; if target has empty history same Validation outcome — defensive against the upstream-history-pruned-out-from-under-the-fork edge case named in ADR-014 §3); `ClosePullRequestUseCase` (checks PR is still OPEN as defense-in-depth + caller is signed in; intentionally does NOT do the "is caller author or target owner" check — that lives at the UI layer in `PullRequestDetailViewModel.canClose` so the use case doesn't need to take a `PatternRepository` dependency for a check the server-side RLS UPDATE policy already enforces; KDoc names the offline-local-write window per the codebase-wide `Repository.close` precedent so future readers understand the offline-tolerance contract). All 5 use cases use the project's standard `try { ... } catch (e: CancellationException) { throw e } catch (e: Exception) { e.toUseCaseError() }` envelope per the Phase 36.3 / 37.x precedent. **`PullRequestRepository` interface extension**: 2 new methods `subscribeToCommentsChannel(prId)` + `closeCommentsChannel()` to manage the dynamic per-PR Realtime channel `pull-request-comments-<prId>` per ADR-014 §7 — implementation in `PullRequestRepositoryImpl` mirrors the Phase 4b `CommentRepositoryImpl` pattern with internal `commentsChannel: ChannelHandle?` + `subscribedPrId: String?` + `channelMutex: Mutex` for serialization. Idempotent on the same prId via the `commentsChannel != null && subscribedPrId == prId` short-circuit inside the mutex; channel-swap branch when prId changes (defensive against in-flight init re-entry; ViewModel is parameterized on prId so this is mostly a guard rail). Subscribe-then-fetch pattern: opens the channel via `provider.createChannel("pull-request-comments-$prId")`, registers the postgres-change Flow with `ChangeFilter("pull_request_id", prId)`, calls `subscribe()`, THEN fires a best-effort remote `getCommentsForPullRequest` to seed the cache — failure here is tolerated (KDoc explicit), the local cache stays whatever it was and Realtime fills the gap as events arrive. `handleCommentAction` exhaustively routes the 4 PostgresAction variants: INSERT → `local.upsertComment(comment)`; UPDATE / DELETE / SELECT silent no-op since RLS forbids those actions server-side. New ctor params `channelProvider: RealtimeChannelProvider? = null` + `scope: CoroutineScope? = null` are nullable with default-null so test fakes that construct the impl directly stay valid AND local-only mode (no Supabase) keeps both methods as silent no-ops. **`PullRequestDetailViewModel`** parameterized on `prId: String`. State carries `pullRequest: PullRequest?`, `comments: List<PullRequestComment>`, `users: Map<String, User>`, `targetOwnerId: String?` (resolved via `PatternRepository.getById(targetPatternId)` — explicit try/catch with `CancellationException` rethrow, NOT `runCatching` per code review MEDIUM-1 fix; runCatching swallows CancellationException which would silently null `targetOwnerId` for the session and permanently disable the merge/close gates after a coroutine timeout), `currentUserId: String?`, `commentDraft: String`, `isLoading`, `isSendingComment`, `isClosingPr`, `pendingCloseConfirmation`, `pendingMergeConfirmation`, `error`. **`canMerge` and `canClose` are derived state-class properties, not top-level extension properties** — moved during iOS build verification because top-level extensions on a Kotlin data class bridge to Swift as `PullRequestDetailViewModelKt.canMerge(state)` (Kt-class function) which xcodebuild rejected with "cannot find type 'PullRequestDetailViewModelKt' in scope"; making them inline `get()` properties on the data class lets the Swift bridge read them as plain `Bool` getters via `state.canMerge` / `state.canClose`. `canMerge` = `pr.status == OPEN && currentUserId == targetOwnerId` (Phase 38.3 keeps the merge button visually disabled regardless; gate computed centrally so 38.4 just enables the screen-side `enabled` flag). `canClose` = `status == OPEN && (currentUserId == authorId || currentUserId == targetOwnerId)` per ADR-014 §1 "either party may close". **Realtime lifecycle**: `init` block sequences (1) `subscribeToCommentsChannel(prId)` BEFORE seeding the comment list so any INSERT landing during the seed window propagates through the channel rather than being missed, then (2) sync `currentUserId` from `authRepository.getCurrentUserId()`, then (3) `loadInitial()` (PR + target pattern + user resolution), then (4) `observeComments()` for live updates. `onCleared` spawns a detached `CoroutineScope(Dispatchers.Default + NonCancellable).launch { withTimeout(5_000) { closeCommentsChannel() } }` — `viewModelScope` is already cancelled by the time `onCleared` runs so a plain `viewModelScope.launch` would be dropped. `NonCancellable` ensures an external cancel signal cannot race the cleanup; `withTimeout(5_000)` bounds the lifetime so a hung Realtime `unsubscribe` (server timeout, network partition) cannot leak the scope indefinitely. 5s is generous for a websocket unsubscribe round-trip; the cleanup is idempotent on the server side so a forced timeout is safe. This pattern was the load-bearing fix from code review HIGH-1 (the original `CoroutineScope(Dispatchers.Default).launch { }` with no timeout could leak the scope forever if `closeCommentsChannel` never returned). **`observePrRow` flow**: subscribes to `getPullRequest.observe(prId, ownerId, scope)` and pipes fresh emissions into `_state.pullRequest` so a status flip landing through Realtime (close echo, merge echo) lands without a manual refresh. The `.catch { e -> if (e is CancellationException) throw e else _state.update { ... error = ... } }` re-throws CancellationException per code review LOW-1 fix — the prior version surfaced job cancellation as a user-visible Snackbar error which is wrong. Same fix applied to `observeComments`'s `.catch`. **Optimistic post-comment cache write**: `postCommentInternal` adds the freshly-posted comment to `_state.comments` immediately on success (idempotent — checks `comments.any { it.id == result.value.id }` first) so the user sees their post even in local-only mode where the Realtime echo never arrives. Resolves the just-posted comment's author via `resolveUsersForComments` so the row renders with the correct display name on first paint. **One-shot navigation channel**: `_navEvents: Channel<PullRequestDetailNavEvent>(Channel.BUFFERED)` carries `PrClosed` after a successful close so the screen can surface the `message_pr_closed_successfully` Snackbar (Compose) / 2-second `.overlay` toast (iOS) without blocking the close callback. **Compose `PullRequestDetailScreen`**: Scaffold + TopAppBar (back button + `title_pull_request_detail` + status chip via private `PullRequestStatus.labelKey: StringResource` extension mirroring the 38.2 PR-list pattern). LazyColumn body holds `TitleAndStatus` (PR title + author line `label_pr_authored_by` parametric + timestamp), `DescriptionCard` (only renders when `pr.description?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }`), `DiffPreviewCard` ("View proposed changes" Button routing to the existing Phase 37.3 `ChartDiffScreen` between `pr.commonAncestorRevisionId` and `pr.sourceTipRevisionId` — **inline diff render deferred** per the same scope-cut precedent as Phase 36.4 iOS Discovery thumbnail; extracting `DualCanvasPanel` from ChartDiffScreen into a thumbnail-sized component is a meaningful refactor of the gestural Compose Canvas that's out of scope for 38.3, the `prDiffPreview` testTag is reserved for the future inline-render surface), `label_pr_comments` section header, `CommentRow` per comment (author name + timestamp + body, Surface card layout matching the 38.2 PR-list visual rhythm). `CommentComposeBox` (OutlinedTextField + post Button, `enabled = !isSending`, post button additionally `&& draft.isNotBlank()`) renders below the LazyColumn only when `pr.status == OPEN`. `ActionBar` renders below the compose box when `canMerge || canClose`: target owner sees "Merge" Button (visually disabled for 38.3) + "Close" TextButton; source author sees just "Close". testTags per ADR-014 §6: `pullRequestDetailScreen` (root), `prTitleLabel`, `prDescriptionLabel`, `prDiffPreview`, `commentInputField`, `postCommentButton`, `mergeButton`, `closeButton`, `commentRow_<commentId>`. Phase 38.3 also adds the merge/close confirmation `AlertDialog`s — close dialog confirms via `ConfirmClose` event; merge dialog confirm button is `enabled = false` (the body text explains the deferral) so even a user who taps "Merge" still sees the "Coming in Phase 38.4" rationale rather than nothing. **NavGraph**: new `@Serializable data class PullRequestDetail(val prId: String)` route. The 38.2 `composable<PullRequestList>` block's `onPullRequestClick = { _ -> }` no-op pivots to `{ prId -> navController.navigate(PullRequestDetail(prId = prId)) }`. New `composable<PullRequestDetail>` block plumbs `onOpenDiff = { baseRevisionId, targetRevisionId -> navController.navigate(ChartDiff(...)) }`. **iOS mirror** at `iosApp/iosApp/Screens/PullRequestDetailScreen.swift` uses the established `ScopedViewModel<PullRequestDetailViewModel, PullRequestDetailState>` holder pattern. Body uses `ContentUnavailableView` for the not-found branch, `ScrollView { VStack { ... } }` for the loaded branch (header + description + diff preview + comments section), `commentComposeBox` HStack at the bottom only when `pr.status == .open`, `actionBar` HStack below when `canMerge || canClose`. SwiftUI `.confirmationDialog` for both close (destructive button) and merge (confirm button `.disabled(true)` per the deferral) — `Binding<Bool>` derived from `state.pendingCloseConfirmation` / `state.pendingMergeConfirmation` so the dialog dismissal routes through the matching ViewModel event. `navEvents` Closeable observed in `.task` and closed in `.onDisappear` per the established Phase 32.2 / 36.5 iOS Closeable leak audit pattern; the `PrClosed` event triggers a 2-second `.overlay(alignment: .bottom)` toast carrying `message_pr_closed_successfully`. The diff-preview "View proposed changes" Button routes via `path.append(Route.chartDiff(...))`. **Existing `PullRequestListScreen.swift` updated**: signature gains `path: Binding<NavigationPath>`; row tap pivots from no-op comment to `path.append(Route.pullRequestDetail(prId: pr.id))`. **`PullRequestStatus` Swift enum bridging**: same `default: return status.name` fallback in `statusKey` per the Phase 33.1.13 precedent — locale-neutral non-empty fallback so a future enum addition without matching Swift switch update surfaces visibly at runtime. **Date formatting**: inline pattern `Date(timeIntervalSince1970: TimeInterval(epochSeconds))` matches existing `PullRequestListScreen.swift` / `ChartHistoryScreen.swift` precedent — initially used `Kotlinx_datetimeInstant` typed parameter but xcodebuild couldn't resolve the type from the bridged Shared framework so refactored to take `Int64` directly. **iOS bridge**: `KoinHelper.kt` adds `getPullRequestDetailViewModel(prId)` accessor + `wrapPullRequestDetailState` (StateFlow → FlowWrapper) + `wrapPullRequestDetailNavEvents` (Flow → EventFlowWrapper). `ViewModelFactory.swift` adds `pullRequestDetailViewModel(prId:)`. `AppRouter.swift` adds `Route.pullRequestDetail(prId: String)` with Hashable conformance + destinationView mapping. `xcodegen generate` regenerated `iosApp.xcodeproj` to register `PullRequestDetailScreen.swift`. **Koin DI**: `UseCaseModule` registers all 5 new factories. `ViewModelModule` registers `PullRequestDetailViewModel` with all 9 dependencies (5 use cases + 4 repos). `RepositoryModule` `PullRequestRepositoryImpl` registration extended with `channelProvider = getOrNull<RealtimeChannelProvider>()` + `scope = getOrNull<CoroutineScope>(applicationScopeQualifier)` so local-only mode keeps the `subscribeToCommentsChannel` call as a silent no-op rather than throwing on missing Supabase. **i18n** — 14 new keys across all 5 sources (325 total, +14 from 311 baseline; matches the ADR §6 budget exactly): `title_pull_request_detail`, `label_pr_description`, `label_pr_diff_preview`, `label_pr_comments`, `hint_add_comment_to_pr` (with U+2026 ellipsis per convention), `action_post_comment`, `action_merge_pr`, `action_close_pr`, `dialog_merge_pr_title`, `dialog_merge_pr_body` (body explicitly names "Conflict resolution ships in Phase 38.4" so users tapping the disabled merge button see the rationale), `dialog_close_pr_title`, `dialog_close_pr_body`, `state_pr_not_found`, `message_pr_closed_successfully`. Reuses 38.2 / 38.1 `action_back` / `action_cancel` / `title_error` / `action_ok` / `label_someone` / `label_pr_authored_by` / `label_pr_status_{open,merged,closed}`. `message_pr_merged_successfully` is deferred to 38.4 because that's where the merge UX lands; 38.3 only ships the close feedback message. **`FakePullRequestRepository` test fake widened** from "read-side only" to cover `getById` / comment Flows / `openPullRequest` / `closePullRequest` / `postComment` / `subscribeToCommentsChannel` / `closeCommentsChannel` so the new use cases can be exercised end-to-end. New affordances: `seedById` / `setComments` for arrange-phase setup; `lastOpened` / `lastClosed` / `lastPosted` / `subscribeCount` / `closeCount` / `lastSubscribedPrId` for assert-phase verification; `nextGetByIdError` / `nextOpenError` / `nextCloseError` / `nextPostCommentError` / `nextGetCommentsError` for failure-path coverage. **Tests (+44 commonTest, 1087 → 1131)**: `GetPullRequestUseCaseTest` (6 tests) covers cached-success, NotFound, exception → Failure, observe-from-incoming-flow, observe-id-filter, observe-status-flip-on-Realtime-emission. `GetPullRequestCommentsUseCaseTest` (4 tests) covers seeded list, empty cache, exception, observe Flow. `PostPullRequestCommentUseCaseTest` (6 tests) covers happy path with body trimming, blank-body Validation, max-length Validation, unauthenticated Authentication, repo-error Unknown wrapping, fresh-id-per-call (idempotent INSERT-OR-IGNORE on remote needs distinct UUIDs to avoid silent coalesce). `OpenPullRequestUseCaseTest` (9 tests) — the most extensive coverage given the parent-chain walk algorithm: source-tip-is-fork-point, walk-back-multiple-steps, no-ancestor-Validation, empty-target-history-Validation, blank-title-Validation, max-title-Validation, unauthenticated-Authentication, blank-description-stored-as-null, repo-write-recorded. `ClosePullRequestUseCaseTest` (5 tests) — happy path, already-merged Validation, already-closed Validation, unauthenticated Authentication, repo-error wrapping. `PullRequestDetailViewModelTest` (14 tests) — load-PR-plus-target-owner-plus-comments, NotFound surfacing, exactly-one channel subscribe call, canMerge true for target owner, canMerge false for source author, canClose true for source author, canClose false for unrelated user, canClose false on merged PR, CommentDraftChanged, PostComment writes through and clears draft, RequestClose-then-ConfirmClose flips status + emits PrClosed nav event, DismissCloseConfirmation no-ops the dialog without closing, ClearError, comment-author display name resolution. New private `FakeRevisionRepoForOpenPr` test class (in `OpenPullRequestUseCaseTest.kt`) implements the `ChartRevisionRepository` interface with seeded `getHistoryForPattern(patternId)` + `getRevision(revisionId)` lookups; other methods throw to surface accidental reach. Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 1 HIGH / 1 MEDIUM / 2 LOW first pass — all 4 fixed pre-commit. **HIGH** (`onCleared` detached coroutine scope leak risk — original `CoroutineScope(Dispatchers.Default).launch { closeCommentsChannel() }` had no timeout and no NonCancellable, so a hung Realtime unsubscribe could leak the scope indefinitely with no mechanism to cancel) fixed by adding `+ NonCancellable` to the scope context AND wrapping the `closeCommentsChannel` call with `withTimeout(5_000)`. **MEDIUM** (`runCatching { patternRepository.getById(...) }.getOrNull()` swallows CancellationException, which silently nulls `targetOwnerId` for the session — the merge gate is load-bearing on this field so a coroutine-cancelled timeout would permanently disable the merge button until the user re-enters the screen) fixed by replacing with explicit try/catch that rethrows CancellationException per the Phase 36.3 / 37.x precedent. **LOW-1** (`.catch` operator in `observePrRow` and `observeComments` swallows CancellationException and surfaces it as a user-visible Snackbar error) fixed by adding `if (e is CancellationException) throw e` at the top of both `.catch` lambdas. **LOW-2** (`runCatching` in `resolveUsersForPr` and `resolveUsersForComments`) refactored to explicit try/catch for consistency with the project-wide pattern even though display-name resolution failure is non-fatal. **LOW-3** (`ClosePullRequestUseCase` KDoc missing offline-local-write window disclosure) addressed by adding an "Offline-local-write window" paragraph to the use case's KDoc explicitly naming the codebase-wide offline-tolerance contract. **Kover exclusion**: `PullRequestDetailScreenKt*` added to the screen-level Compose UI exclusion list. **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1131 tests, +44 from 1087 baseline — overshoots the ADR §8's +20–25 target but the overshoot is concentrated in `OpenPullRequestUseCaseTest`'s 9 tests where the parent-chain walk algorithm needs careful coverage of every branch including the source-tip-is-fork-point shortcut and the empty-target-history defensive path), `:shared:koverVerify`, `bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` (325 keys). iOS app builds via `xcodebuild -project iosApp.xcodeproj -scheme iosApp -destination 'generic/platform=iOS Simulator' -configuration Debug build` ✅. **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-014 §6**: merge button stays inert (Phase 38.4 wires the SECURITY DEFINER `merge_pull_request` RPC + `MergePullRequestUseCase` + `ConflictDetector` algorithm + `ChartConflictResolutionScreen`); inline diff canvas render deferred (the "View proposed changes" link routes to existing Phase 37.3 ChartDiffScreen, extracting a thumbnail-sized component is a meaningful refactor — same scope-cut precedent as Phase 36.4 iOS Discovery thumbnail); ChartViewer overflow "Open pull request" entry deferred (would need to lift `parentPatternId` + `visibility` from the chart load path into ChartViewerViewModel state + add a compose-form-and-submit flow over `OpenPullRequestUseCase`; the data layer + use case are wired and ready, but the UI flow is its own slice — likely 38.3.1 if it lands ahead of 38.4); Maestro E2E deferred — same linked-pattern + open-PR fixture prerequisite as Phase 38.2 + needs Supabase connectivity for the Realtime channel test. **Forward-compat anchors for 38.4**: `canMerge` already gated on `pr.status == OPEN && currentUserId == targetOwnerId` and rendered visually disabled — Phase 38.4 just removes the `enabled = false` flag on the merge button + wires the confirm button to `MergePullRequestUseCase`. The merge confirmation dialog UI ships in 38.3 with the body copy explaining the deferral so the user-facing wiring is end-to-end ready.

- **Phase 38.2**: Pull request read-only list (ADR-014 §6, §8) — second code slice of Phase 38 wires the data spine from 38.1 into a user-visible read surface. **Use cases**: `GetIncomingPullRequestsUseCase` + `GetOutgoingPullRequestsUseCase` symmetric — both expose `observe(ownerId): Flow<List<PullRequest>>` that delegates to `PullRequestRepository.observeIncomingForOwner` / `observeOutgoingForOwner` (local-only flows per the repository's KDoc) plus a one-shot `suspend operator fun invoke(ownerId): UseCaseResult<List<PullRequest>>` that backfills the cache from the remote. Both use the standard `try { ... } catch (e: CancellationException) { throw e } catch (e: Exception) { e.toUseCaseError() }` envelope per the Phase 36.3 / 37.3 / 37.4 precedent. Repository ctor param is non-null because `PullRequestRepository` is unconditionally registered in `RepositoryModule` (it handles local-only mode internally via `remote = null`), matching `GetChartHistoryUseCase`'s precedent. **`PullRequestListViewModel`** parameterized on `defaultFilter: PullRequestFilter` (a new top-level `@Serializable enum class` with INCOMING / OUTGOING — `@Serializable` so the route can carry it). State carries `filter: PullRequestFilter`, `pullRequests: List<PullRequest>`, `users: Map<String, User>` (resolved post-list-load via `UserRepository.getByIds` — same pattern as `ActivityFeedViewModel.resolveUsers`), `isLoading`, `error`. Filter switching via `_filter: MutableStateFlow<PullRequestFilter>` + `flatMapLatest` — `SelectFilter` event flips `_filter.value` (and resets `users = emptyMap()` so a stale author entry from the old filter cannot bleed into the new one via `resolveUsers`'s dedup-by-key skip). **Cold-launch seeding contract embedded inside `flatMapLatest`** — the prior `viewModelScope.launch { ... }` for the seed escaped `flatMapLatest`'s cancellable scope and could surface the prior filter's error after the user had already switched (caught by code review HIGH-1; fixed by moving the seed inside a single `flow { val seed = ...; emitAll(observe(...)) }` block so seed and observe share lifetime). **`resolveUsers` race fix** (code review HIGH-2): the prior version captured `currentUsers = _state.value.users` BEFORE the `userRepository.getByIds` suspend, then merged via `currentUsers + resolved` AFTER, which silently dropped concurrent resolutions when two `onEach` emissions arrived back-to-back under network pressure. Fixed by reading inside `_state.update { current -> current.copy(users = current.users + resolved) }` so the merge always sees the latest accumulated map; `ActivityFeedViewModel.resolveUsers` carries the same race but is left unfixed in this slice (Tech Debt note inline). **Compose `PullRequestListScreen`** — Scaffold with TopAppBar (back button + title `title_pull_requests`), `FilterChipRow` between header and list (with `incomingFilterChip` / `outgoingFilterChip` testTags), main body groups PRs by `STATUS_DISPLAY_ORDER = listOf(OPEN, MERGED, CLOSED)` so OPEN PRs always render first regardless of created_at ordering. Each `PullRequestRow` shows: title + status chip on first line (parametric `prTitleLabel_<id>` / `prStatusChip_<id>` testTags), author line `label_pr_authored_by` parametric (`%1$s` resolves to `state.users[pr.authorId]?.displayName ?: stringResource(label_someone)`), and a timestamp via the existing `Instant.formatFull()` helper. Tap on a row routes through `onPullRequestClick` which is wired as no-op for 38.2 — Phase 38.3 will route to `PullRequestDetailScreen`. Status chip uses `AssistChip` with `enabled = false` + `disabledLabelColor = onSurface` for static rendering. Empty state surfaces `state_no_pull_requests` headline + `state_no_pull_requests_body` description. Root testTag `pullRequestListScreen`. **Status enum extension** `PullRequestStatus.labelKey: StringResource` with exhaustive `when` on the 3 cases — `OPEN → label_pr_status_open`, `MERGED → label_pr_status_merged`, `CLOSED → label_pr_status_closed` (private to the screen file; promote to `ui/components/` if a second consumer surfaces, same pattern as Phase 33.1.10's `Difficulty.labelKey` promotion). **NavGraph** new `@Serializable data class PullRequestList(val defaultFilter: PullRequestFilter)` route + `composable<PullRequestList>` block; the `PullRequestFilter` enum routes through kotlinx-serialization natively without any ordinal-int conversion. **iOS mirror** at `iosApp/iosApp/Screens/PullRequestListScreen.swift` uses the established `ScopedViewModel<PullRequestListViewModel, PullRequestListState>` holder pattern. SwiftUI body uses `ContentUnavailableView` for empty state, `List(ordered, id: \.id)` body, custom `FilterChipButton` private struct for selectable chip rendering (Capsule background + accent overlay; `accessibilityIdentifier` parameter for `incomingFilterChip` / `outgoingFilterChip` parity), `PullRequestStatusBadge` private struct for the status chip (renamed from initial `StatusBadge` per code review fix — collision with the project-status `StatusBadge` already defined in `ProjectListScreen.swift`). `statusKey` private property uses `default: return status.name` per the Phase 33.1.13 `SharedContentScreen.swift` `Difficulty` precedent — locale-neutral non-empty fallback so a future `PullRequestStatus` addition without a matching Swift switch update surfaces visibly at runtime rather than silently mislabeled as "Open". **Entry points**: (a) `ProjectListScreen` (Compose) gains an `onSuggestionsClick` callback wired through NavGraph to `navigate(PullRequestList(defaultFilter = INCOMING))`; toolbar IconButton uses `Icons.Default.Forum` with `action_pull_requests` contentDescription (NEW key, distinct from `title_pull_requests` per the role-prefix discipline established in Phase 33.1.3 — toolbar action vs screen title can diverge in JA, with the JA value `プルリクエストを開く` carrying the verb suffix for natural TalkBack announcement). testTag `pullRequestsButton`. (b) `ProjectListScreen.swift` mirror gains the same Menu item with `action_pull_requests` label + `pullRequestsButton` accessibilityIdentifier. (c) `ProjectDetailScreen` `PatternInfoSection` (both Compose + SwiftUI) gains a new "Pull Requests" link beneath the existing chart-related links — surfaces unconditionally; the default-filter selection happens at the outer screen layer via `pattern.parentPatternId != null ? OUTGOING : INCOMING` (forks default to Outgoing; upstream patterns default to Incoming) per ADR-014 §6. testTag `openPullRequestsLink`. **iOS bridge**: `KoinHelper.kt` adds `getPullRequestListViewModel(defaultFilter: PullRequestFilter)` accessor + `wrapPullRequestListState`. `ViewModelFactory.swift` adds `pullRequestListViewModel(defaultFilter:)`. `AppRouter.swift` adds `Route.pullRequestList(defaultFilter: PullRequestFilter)` with Hashable conformance and `destinationView` mapping. `xcodegen generate` regenerated `iosApp.xcodeproj` to register `PullRequestListScreen.swift`. **Author display name resolution**: 38.2 reuses `UserRepository.getByIds` which is already wired through `RepositoryModule` (consumed by `ActivityFeedViewModel`, `SharedWithMeViewModel`, `ProjectDetailViewModel` since Phase 36.5). Fallback to `label_someone` when the lookup misses (cold-launch with empty UserRepository cache, account deleted via ON DELETE SET NULL, or null `authorId` on the PR row itself). **i18n** — 10 new keys across all 5 sources (311 total, +10 from 301 baseline; ADR §6 budget called for 9, the +1 for `action_pull_requests` was added during code review per the role-prefix discipline): `title_pull_requests`, `action_pull_requests` (toolbar IconButton + iOS menu Label), `label_filter_incoming`, `label_filter_outgoing`, `state_no_pull_requests`, `state_no_pull_requests_body`, `label_pr_status_open`, `label_pr_status_merged`, `label_pr_status_closed`, `label_pr_authored_by` parametric (`%1$s` EN / `%1$s` JA / `%1$@` xcstrings — JA reads `<name>が作成` for natural grammar). Reuses `action_back` / `title_error` / `action_ok` / `label_someone`. **Tests (+22 commonTest, 1065 → 1087)**: `GetIncomingPullRequestsUseCaseTest` (5 tests) covers seeded list, empty cache, exception → Failure, observe Flow seeded, ownerId scoping. `GetOutgoingPullRequestsUseCaseTest` (5 tests) symmetric — same shape, distinct fake state to verify the outgoing path. `PullRequestListViewModelTest` (12 tests) covers default INCOMING + OUTGOING load, SelectFilter switches list and clears users, no-op SelectFilter on same filter, repo flow live emission, unauthenticated error path, user display name resolution, all-null-authorIds keeps users empty, ClearError, ownerId-scoping, seed-failure error surface (validates the HIGH-1 flatMapLatest fix), filter-switch users-clear (validates the MEDIUM-1 stale-users-bleed fix). New shared test fake `FakePullRequestRepository` implementing the full `PullRequestRepository` interface — read-side methods backed by per-ownerId `MutableStateFlow<List<PullRequest>>` so observe Flows stay live across `setIncoming` / `setOutgoing` calls; write-side methods (open / close / postComment / getCommentsFor / getById) `error("Not used by Phase 38.2 use cases")` to surface accidental cross-test reach. Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 2 HIGH / 4 MEDIUM / 3 LOW first pass — HIGHs (escaped seed coroutine, stale `currentUsers` snapshot in `resolveUsers`) + MEDIUMs (stale users-map across filter switch, `title_pull_requests`-as-contentDescription role-prefix violation, iOS `default: return "label_pr_status_open"` silent mislabel, missing seed-failure regression test) + 1 LOW (outgoing scoping test parity) all addressed pre-commit. The remaining 2 LOWs were pre-existing inconsistencies (GetChartHistoryUseCase missing `CancellationException` rethrow; iOS alert dismiss button uses bare `String` literal that auto-promotes through SwiftUI overload resolution) — neither created by 38.2; flagged for separate sweep. **Kover exclusion**: `PullRequestListScreenKt*` added to the screen-level Compose UI exclusion list. **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1087 tests, +22 from 1065 baseline — comfortably above the +10 ADR §8 budget; the bump is from the ViewModel surface needing more state-transition coverage than the ADR estimated, plus the LOW-3 outgoing scoping test parity), `:shared:koverVerify`, `bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` (311 keys). iOS app builds via `xcodebuild -project iosApp.xcodeproj -scheme iosApp -destination 'generic/platform=iOS Simulator' -configuration Debug build` ✅. **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-014 §6**: unread badge with last-seen-at tracking deferred to Phase 38.3 (the `countOpenIncomingForOwner` SQLDelight query is wired and ready, but the client-side last-seen-at storage + Badge composable land alongside the read-state mechanism); per-row tap routing to `PullRequestDetailScreen` is Phase 38.3; PR open / merge / comment flows are 38.3 / 38.4. Maestro E2E deferred — flow needs a pre-seeded PR fixture which adds significant Maestro setup with no clear value gain over the 22 ViewModel + use-case tests; reopen if Phase 38.3 surfaces a real interaction-flow regression. **Forward-compat anchors for 38.3**: the `onPullRequestClick: (String) -> Unit` callback is already plumbed through `PullRequestListScreen` + `PullRequestListScreen.swift` (currently no-op) so Phase 38.3 just changes the NavGraph wiring `{ _ -> }` → `{ navController.navigate(PullRequestDetail(prId = it)) }` without touching the screen layer.

- **Phase 38.1**: Pull request data spine (ADR-014 §1, §2, §3, §5, §7) — first code slice of Phase 38, lands the schema + domain + repository + sync + Realtime plumbing without any UI surface. Sets up `pull_requests` and `pull_request_comments` as new sibling tables alongside `chart_revisions`/`chart_branches` from Phase 37.1, plus the `merge_pull_request` SECURITY DEFINER RPC that's the only writer permitted to produce `chart_revisions.author_id != owner_id` rows. **Migration 016** (`016_pull_requests.sql`): `pull_requests` table with FKs to `patterns(id) ON DELETE CASCADE` on both source + target sides, FKs to `chart_branches(id) ON DELETE CASCADE` on both branch sides, and FKs to `chart_revisions(revision_id) ON DELETE RESTRICT` on `source_tip_revision_id` + `common_ancestor_revision_id` (matching the ADR-013 §1 standalone-UNIQUE FK target precedent — `revision_id` is the canonical commit identifier per ADR-008 §6). `merged_revision_id` FK uses `ON DELETE SET NULL` because chart_revisions are immutable (no DELETE policy in migration 015) and the merge result reference can dangle gracefully. `status TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'open' CHECK (status IN ('open', 'merged', 'closed'))` is the closed enum (no DRAFT for v1). Partial unique index `WHERE status = 'open'` on `(source_branch_id, target_branch_id)` is INSERT-side only — prevents duplicate OPEN rows for the same branch pair, but allows close-and-reopen indefinitely (the closed rows accumulate; that's the correct audit-trail behavior). Three indexes for the list-screen hot paths: `(target_pattern_id, status, created_at DESC)`, `(source_pattern_id, status, created_at DESC)`, `(author_id, status)`. RLS: SELECT readable by author OR target owner; INSERT requires `author_id = auth.uid() AND source_pattern_id IN (...patterns I own)` plus the **load-bearing** `AND source_pattern_id IN (SELECT id FROM patterns WHERE parent_pattern_id = target_pattern_id)` clause that enforces the v1 fork-routing invariant — without it, an authenticated user could open a PR from any pattern they own against any target pattern UUID. UPDATE policy permits status flips by either party, with `WITH CHECK status IN ('open', 'closed')` so the merge transition (→ 'merged') is reachable only via the SECURITY DEFINER RPC. No DELETE policy — PRs are kept as audit trail, CASCADE on pattern deletion is the only cleanup path. `pull_request_comments` table similar shape: append-only, `length(body) <= 5000` CHECK, RLS gates on PR-participant set. **`merge_pull_request` SECURITY DEFINER RPC** (~70 lines plpgsql): validates PR exists, status='open', caller is target owner (`SELECT 1 FROM patterns WHERE id = v_pr.target_pattern_id AND owner_id = v_caller`); validates strategy in `('squash', 'fast_forward')`; validates source tip unchanged via `SELECT tip_revision_id FROM chart_branches WHERE id = v_pr.source_branch_id` against `v_pr.source_tip_revision_id` (drift = `RAISE EXCEPTION 'Source tip drifted; re-resolve required'`); captures `v_target_tip_pre_merge` from `chart_branches WHERE id = v_pr.target_branch_id` BEFORE the INSERT (HIGH-1 fix from ADR review — without this, the chart_documents UPDATE's subquery against the just-inserted row would silently zero out `parent_revision_id` if the row went missing for any reason); INSERTs the merged revision into `chart_revisions` with `author_id = v_pr.author_id` + `owner_id = v_caller`, threading `v_target_tip_pre_merge` as the new revision's `parent_revision_id` and using `RETURNING parent_revision_id INTO v_inserted_parent_revision_id` to verify the row actually landed (defensive; raises if `IS DISTINCT FROM v_target_tip_pre_merge`). Then UPDATEs `chart_branches.tip_revision_id` for target, UPDATEs `chart_documents` tip pointer for the target pattern, marks PR `status='merged' + merged_revision_id + merged_at = now()`. **Concurrency model**: `FOR UPDATE` on the PR row at the function start serializes concurrent merges — the second caller blocks until the first commits then sees `status='merged'` and bails on the "PR not open" check. The partial unique index prevents duplicate INSERT-side OPEN rows, NOT the merge race; these two mechanisms are complementary, not redundant. Same shape as `delete_own_account` from Phase 17 / ADR-005 — `REVOKE ALL ON FUNCTION ... FROM public; GRANT EXECUTE ... TO authenticated`. Both new tables added to `supabase_realtime` publication. **SQLDelight schemas**: `PullRequest.sq` mirrors the Postgres table with `TEXT` columns + INSERT-OR-REPLACE upsert (PR carries its own `(created_at, updated_at)` timestamps, sync layer treats INSERT and UPDATE both as upsert per ADR-014 §7) + 3 indexes mirroring the Postgres ones. Queries: `getById` / `getByTargetPattern` / `getBySourcePattern` / `getIncomingForOwner` (INNER JOIN on `PatternEntity` to scope by `owner_id` locally — RLS does the same server-side) / `getOutgoingForOwner` / paired observers + `countOpenIncomingForOwner` (Phase 38.2 unread badge) / `upsert` / `updateStatus` (close path) / `deleteById` / `deleteByPatternId` (CASCADE backfill — clears where source OR target matches; called with the same id passed twice to match `WHERE source_pattern_id = ? OR target_pattern_id = ?`). `PullRequestComment.sq`: append-only INSERT OR IGNORE upsert (rather than INSERT OR REPLACE — comments are immutable at RLS so a slightly-different copy arriving via Realtime echo should NOT silently overwrite). Both `.sq` files paired with `6.sqm` containing the SQLite migration. ON DELETE CASCADE on both pattern FKs at SQLite layer + on `pull_request_id` in comments. **Domain**: `PullRequest` data class (Serializable, `@SerialName` mappings) with `mergedRevisionId` / `mergedAt` / `closedAt` nullable + `authorId` nullable per ON DELETE SET NULL contract. `PullRequestStatus` enum (OPEN/MERGED/CLOSED) with `@SerialName("open")` / `("merged")` / `("closed")` matching the Postgres CHECK values verbatim. `PullRequest.canMerge(currentUserId, targetOwnerId)` extension method = `status == OPEN && currentUserId == targetOwnerId` — UI-affordance-only gate; the RPC's `WHERE owner_id = v_caller` clause is the actual security boundary (KDoc explicit about caller-supplies-correct-targetOwnerId contract). `PullRequestComment` data class (immutable, append-only). **Mappers**: `PullRequestMapper.kt` — `PullRequestEntity.toDomain()` + `PullRequestCommentEntity.toDomain()` + exhaustive `String.toPullRequestStatus()` (3-way `when` with hard `error()` for unknown wire values — defensive against future migrations adding a 4th status, hard fail beats silent fall-through to OPEN) + `PullRequestStatus.toDbString()` (3-way `when`, no else). **Repository**: `PullRequestRepository` interface ships 11 methods covering Phase 38.2/38.3 read-side + Phase 38.1 write-side. **Merge is NOT a repository method** per ADR-014 §5 — Phase 38.4 wires the RPC through a dedicated `MergePullRequestUseCase` that bypasses the local-then-sync orchestration (the RPC is the only writer permitted to produce author_id != owner_id rows; the caller cannot pre-write a stub locally and reconcile, so the standard local-first pattern doesn't apply). `PullRequestRepositoryImpl` follows the local-first / remote-fallback / sync-or-enqueue pattern from `ChartRevisionRepositoryImpl`. `closePullRequest` preserves a caller-supplied `closedAt` if present (idempotent re-close) and stamps a fresh `updatedAt = Clock.System.now()`. `observeIncomingForOwner`/`observeOutgoingForOwner` are local-only flows — KDoc explicitly documents the cold-launch seeding contract: callers should invoke `getIncomingForOwner` first to backfill the cache, then collect this Flow for live updates (Realtime keeps the cache warm thereafter). **Local data source**: `LocalPullRequestDataSource` with `withContext(ioDispatcher)` wrapping every query, separate `prQueries` + `commentQueries` accessors. **Remote data source**: `RemotePullRequestDataSource` implements both `RemotePullRequestSyncOperations` + `RemotePullRequestCommentSyncOperations` — single class, dual interface (matches the Phase 4b sharing precedent where RemoteShare combined ops). `getIncomingForOwner` does a two-step fetch: first the owner's pattern ids via `Columns.raw("id")` projection, then PRs targeting any of them via `isIn("target_pattern_id", patternIds)`. RLS already restricts visibility to participant set, but the explicit pattern-id filter is the semantically-correct "incoming" scope. Two-step is acceptable for 38.1 (no UI consumer yet); when 38.2 hot-path lands, consider promoting to a server-side view or RPC. `upsert` uses `onConflict = "id"` for PR-row idempotency; `appendComment` uses `ignoreDuplicates = true` because comments are immutable at RLS so a re-enqueued append should silently no-op (matches the `RemoteChartRevisionDataSource.append` precedent from Phase 37.1). **Sync wiring**: `SyncEntityType.PULL_REQUEST` + `PULL_REQUEST_COMMENT` enum values added. `SyncExecutor` exhaustively routes both: PR INSERT/UPDATE → `remote.upsert(pr)` (idempotent on id; status → MERGED transitions via the RPC and is NOT enqueued through PendingSync); PR DELETE silent no-op `return true` (PRs are audit trail; SyncManager never enqueues this — defensive fall-through matches `executeChartRevision`'s pattern). PR_COMMENT INSERT → `remote.appendComment(comment)`; UPDATE/DELETE silent no-op (RLS forbids; same precedent). New `RemotePullRequestSyncOperations` + `RemotePullRequestCommentSyncOperations` interfaces in `RemoteSyncOperations.kt` — split into two because the comment surface is append-only and shouldn't carry an `upsert` method, even though the production `RemotePullRequestDataSource` implements both. **Realtime**: `RealtimeSyncManager` gains 6th + 7th channels `pull-requests-incoming-<ownerId>` + `pull-requests-outgoing-<ownerId>` (per ADR-014 §7). Outgoing channel uses `ChangeFilter("author_id", ownerId)` for clean server-side scoping. Incoming channel uses **NO client-side filter** — single-eq `ChangeFilter` cannot express "target_pattern_id IN owned_patterns" (only equality is supported); RLS scopes the broadcast to PRs where the user is participant (author OR target owner) per migration 016. Both channels feed `handlePullRequestAction` which upserts via the local data source. INSERT OR REPLACE on `id` makes the dual-channel delivery idempotent — outgoing PRs get delivered through both the outgoing AND incoming channels (since they pass RLS as participant), causing 2x bandwidth on outgoing events; acceptable for v1 per ADR-014 Negative §2 channel-budget concerns, revisit consolidation if Phase 39 closed beta surfaces a connection cap. DELETE handler uses per-row `deleteById(old.id)` (NOT `deleteByPatternId` like the chart_revisions handler) because a PR sits at the join of two patterns (source + target) and Postgres emits one DELETE event per cascaded PR row — bulk-clear by pattern_id would over-delete; the asymmetry vs chart_revisions is deliberate and documented inline. The dynamic per-PR comments channel `pull-request-comments-<prId>` lands in Phase 38.3 alongside `PullRequestDetailScreen` and is NOT managed by `RealtimeSyncManager` (opened/closed on view lifecycle). `localPullRequest` ctor param is nullable with `null` default + a guard in `subscribe` — keeps existing test call-sites valid. **Koin DI**: `RepositoryModule` registers `LocalPullRequestDataSource` + `RemotePullRequestDataSource` (only when Supabase configured) + `PullRequestRepositoryImpl` as `single<PullRequestRepository>`. `SyncModule` registers both sync-ops aliases pointing at the same `RemotePullRequestDataSource` instance + threads `remotePullRequest` + `remotePullRequestComment` through `SyncExecutor` + threads `localPullRequest` through `RealtimeSyncManager`. **Tests (+32 commonTest, 1033 → 1065 — top of ADR §8's +25–35 target band)**: `PullRequestMapperTest` (6 tests) covers entity round-trip for all 3 statuses + lifecycle timestamps + unknown-status hard-fail + enum<->db exhaustive map + `canMerge` permutations. `PullRequestRepositoryImplTest` (15 tests) covers open/close/post paths, sync enqueue contracts, description + authorId round-trip, case-sensitive id lookup, incoming-vs-outgoing scoping (with seeded `LocalPatternDataSource` for the pattern-owner JOIN), local-only `observeIncomingForOwner` ordering, comment scoping + ascending order, comment INSERT-OR-IGNORE idempotency on Realtime echo, and the MERGED PR Realtime-echo round-trip preserving `mergedRevisionId` + `mergedAt`. `SyncExecutorTest` gains 7 PR-branch tests covering null-remote no-op, INSERT/UPDATE upsert dispatch, DELETE silent no-op, remote-failure propagation for retry, comment INSERT append, and forbidden-comment-UPDATE/DELETE silent-success. `RealtimeSyncManagerPullRequestTest` (4 tests, separate class — doesn't widen the existing test helper signature) covers the 7-channel subscribe count, outgoing `author_id` filter, incoming-no-filter RLS-driven path, and unsubscribe lifecycle. New test fakes: `FakeRemotePullRequestDataSource` implements both sync-ops interfaces with separate fail-flags. Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 1 HIGH / 3 MEDIUM / 2 LOW first pass. **HIGH** (Realtime DELETE handler comment claimed "bulk-clear PRs for the pattern" but the implementation calls `deleteById(old.id)` per-row, creating a documentation/intent mismatch that would mislead a future reader) fixed by rewriting the doc comment to accurately reflect the per-row delete semantics + name the chart_revisions vs PR asymmetry: PRs sit at a join of two patterns so per-row delete is the correct shape, while chart_revisions has a single parent so bulk-clear-by-pattern-id is fine. **MEDIUM-1** (`getIncomingForOwner` two-step remote fetch is N+1-adjacent — first the owner's patterns, then PRs filtered by those ids) acknowledged as acceptable for Phase 38.1 (no UI consumer yet); will become a hot path in Phase 38.2 and merits a server-side view or RPC then. **MEDIUM-2** (no server-side `updated_at` trigger on `pull_requests` — the client clock stamps `updated_at` on close) acknowledged as consistent with how other repositories behave in this codebase (e.g. `ProjectRepositoryImpl`); not a regression. **MEDIUM-3** (`observeIncomingForOwner` is local-only with no remote seed — cold launch with empty cache emits empty list before Realtime backfills) fixed by adding a KDoc note on the interface explicitly documenting the cold-launch seeding contract: callers should invoke `getIncomingForOwner` first. **LOW-1** (`canMerge` doesn't validate that `targetOwnerId` matches `targetPatternId`, trusts the caller — a ViewModel passing the wrong owner id silently flips the gate) fixed by adding a "Caller contract" KDoc paragraph naming the resolution path + the RPC's `WHERE owner_id = v_caller` clause as the actual security boundary. **LOW-2** (Realtime DELETE comment for incoming channel — same root cause as HIGH) addressed via the HIGH fix. **LOW-3** (`assertFalse(... .isNotEmpty())` double-negation in SyncExecutorTest reads awkwardly) fixed by switching to `assertTrue(... .isEmpty())`. **Append-then-update non-atomicity** (ADR-014 Consequences inherited from ADR-013): the merge RPC is atomic server-side via `FOR UPDATE` + transactional `INSERT` + 3 UPDATEs in one function body, so unlike `chart_revisions.append + chart_documents UPDATE` which is two PendingSync entries that can race, the merge transaction either lands fully or doesn't land at all. PR open/close still go through the standard local-then-sync path which has the usual best-effort-eventually-consistent semantics; that's acceptable because PR state is not load-bearing for diff correctness (the RPC re-validates `source_tip_revision_id` against the live tip at merge time and raises if drifted). **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-014 §8**: PR list / detail / merge UI all in 38.2 / 38.3 / 38.4; `MergePullRequestUseCase` (the RPC invocation) in 38.4; conflict detection algorithm + `ChartConflictResolutionScreen` in 38.4; per-PR comments Realtime channel in 38.3. No use cases ship in 38.1 — `PullRequestRepository`'s methods exist but no caller exercises them yet. No i18n keys (data layer; no user-visible surface). Pre-push invariants all green: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1065 tests, +32 from 1033 baseline), `:shared:koverVerify`, `bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` (301 keys, unchanged — 38.1 is data-layer, no i18n surface). **Forward-compat anchors for 38.2**: the local SQLDelight `getIncomingForOwner` query JOINs PatternEntity for owner scoping, so a future "unread badge count" derives from `countOpenIncomingForOwner(ownerId)` directly; the parametric Realtime channels can be filtered locally by status without server-side changes when the unread-mark mechanism lands. 38.3's per-PR comments channel will reuse the existing `ChannelHandle` abstraction with no new infrastructure.

- **Phase 38.0**: ADR-014 cut for pull-request workflow — opens Phase 38 with the data-model + UX shape decided before any code lands. ADR sized at ~1000 lines EN + ~125 line JA summary (matches the ADR-013 EN+JA-summary precedent; bigger than ADR-013's 801 because Phase 38 has more design surface — multi-author writes, RPC atomicity, conflict resolution UI, comment thread, merge strategy). **Key decisions resolved by the agent team**: (1) New `pull_requests` + `pull_request_comments` tables; PR is its own entity with FKs to `patterns` and `chart_branches` on both sides + a `common_ancestor_revision_id` snapshot captured at PR open time. The repurpose-`chart_revisions` alternative was rejected because it conflates commit history with PR routing. (2) Server-side `merge_pull_request` RPC running with `SECURITY DEFINER` is the **only** writer that can produce `author_id != owner_id` rows. ADR-013 deferred RPCs as "revisit if telemetry shows divergence"; Phase 38 is the trigger because Phase 38 needs atomicity that's user-observable, not just "best-effort eventually consistent" like Phase 37's tip pointer. The function takes `FOR UPDATE` on the PR row to serialize concurrent merge attempts; the partial unique index on `(source_branch_id, target_branch_id) WHERE status = 'open'` prevents INSERT-side duplicate OPEN PRs. These two mechanisms are complementary, not redundant. The function precedent is `delete_own_account` from Phase 17 / ADR-005. (3) **Squash is the default merge strategy**. Fast-forward auto-applies when applicable (resolved doc byte-equal to source tip's doc, no target-side divergence) but is detection-only — v1 still produces a 1-parent commit row so the testing surface stays bounded. Multi-parent merge-commit rejected because `chart_revisions.parent_revision_id` is single-valued; supporting it would force a schema redesign. Knitters do not benefit from multi-parent visualization. (4) **New `ChartConflictResolutionScreen`**, NOT a mode of `ChartDiffScreen`. ChartDiffScreen is read-only and 2-pane (base vs target); conflict resolution is interactive and 3-pane (ancestor pinned + theirs vs mine + per-cell picker). Reusing ChartDiffScreen would require adding interaction + a third-pane mode — bigger change than a new screen. The conflict-detection algorithm is a pure 3-way wrapper over the existing Phase 37 §5 cell-level diff (`ConflictDetector(ancestor, theirs, mine): ConflictReport`), shared between platforms. (5) **Approval shape collapses to merge / close**. v1 has no concept of "team" / "collaborator role"; the target owner is the implicit and sole approver, the merge button itself IS the approval action, the close button IS the rejection action. Comments are informational discussion, not gates. Required-approval is post-v1. (6) **One `PullRequestListScreen(filter: Incoming | Outgoing)`** parameterized — same data model, two perspectives. Avoid building two screens. (7) Realtime fan-out grows from 5 → 7 owner-scoped channels (`pull-requests-incoming-<ownerId>` + `pull-requests-outgoing-<ownerId>`) plus a dynamic `pull-request-comments-<prId>` opened only while PullRequestDetailScreen is on screen. (8) **Plain text only** for PR title / description / comments — Markdown rendering is render-target divergence between Compose `Text` and SwiftUI `Text` and there is no shared sanitizer in the codebase; soft 200 / 2000 / 5000 char limits enforced UI-side. **Phase 38 sub-slice plan** (locked in as ADR §8): 38.0 (this ADR, no code) → 38.1 (`pull_requests` + `pull_request_comments` schema, `merge_pull_request` RPC, domain `PullRequest` / `PullRequestStatus` / `PullRequestComment`, `PullRequestRepository` local + remote + impl, sync wiring, Realtime channels — no UI; +25–35 commonTest, migration 016) → 38.2 (`GetIncomingPullRequestsUseCase` / `GetOutgoingPullRequestsUseCase`, `PullRequestListViewModel`, `PullRequestListScreen` Compose+SwiftUI, entry points from ProjectList overflow + ProjectDetail; read-only — no PR open flow yet; +10 commonTest, 9 i18n keys) → 38.3 (`GetPullRequestUseCase`, `GetPullRequestCommentsUseCase`, `PostPullRequestCommentUseCase`, `OpenPullRequestUseCase`, `ClosePullRequestUseCase`, `PullRequestDetailViewModel`, `PullRequestDetailScreen`, "Open PR" entry from ChartViewer overflow on a forked pattern — no merge yet; +20–25 commonTest, 14 i18n keys) → 38.4 (`ConflictDetector` algorithm, `ConflictResolutionViewModel`, `ChartConflictResolutionScreen`, `MergePullRequestUseCase` invoking the RPC, merge wiring from PullRequestDetailScreen "Merge" button; +20 commonTest, 9 i18n keys). Slices 38.2 / 38.3 / 38.4 form a coherent flow: list → detail → merge. Slipping 38.4 out of MVP is acceptable (read-only review with merge gated behind "Coming soon"); slipping 38.3 leaves the list inert; slipping 38.2 leaves the data spine unobservable. **Forward-compat anchors for post-v1**: `author_id` becoming non-trivial sets up multi-author diff blame ("who last touched this cell"); the merge RPC pattern is reusable for any future cross-table atomic write; the conflict-detection helper sits one layer above the diff algorithm so a future "preview merge" affordance reuses it. **Explicitly NOT in Phase 38 MVP**: "Pull from upstream" affordance on a forked chart (Phase 38+; PR flow runs source → target only), required-approval gates / branch protection, cross-fork PR routing (PR target is always `source.parentPatternId` per ADR-012 §1), multi-author diff blame (Phase 38+ build atop populated `author_id`), CRDT concurrent editing (post-v1), cherry-pick / rebase / squash-with-fixup / amend, multi-parent merge-commit, editing past comments, draft PR state, PR templates / saved descriptions, comment reactions, @-mentions + push notifications, markdown / formatted comments, merge-conflict re-resolution after source drift mid-resolution (resolver re-enters with new source tip; v1 surfaces a generic error), in-detail diff at full pan/zoom (the embedded preview links out to the existing Phase 37.3 ChartDiffScreen). Realtime channel count growth from 5 → 7 (+1 dynamic per-PR while detail is open) is bounded; if Phase 39 closed beta surfaces a free-tier connection cap, channels coalesce then. **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 2 HIGH / 3 MEDIUM / 2 LOW first pass — all 7 fixed pre-commit. **HIGH-1** (silent NULL hazard in the merge RPC's `chart_documents` UPDATE — the original subquery `SELECT parent_revision_id FROM chart_revisions WHERE revision_id = v_new_revision_id` would silently return NULL and zero out `chart_documents.parent_revision_id` if the just-INSERTed row went missing for any reason) fixed by capturing the target's pre-merge tip into a local `v_target_tip_pre_merge` BEFORE the INSERT, threading it as the INSERT's `parent_revision_id` value, and using `INSERT ... RETURNING parent_revision_id INTO v_inserted_parent_revision_id` to verify the row landed; the chart_documents UPDATE then reads the local directly with no subquery dependency. **HIGH-2** (concurrency model documentation — the `FOR UPDATE` lock on the PR row is what prevents double-merge race, NOT the partial unique index which is INSERT-side only) fixed by adding an explicit "Concurrency model" paragraph in §5 of the ADR before the SECURITY DEFINER paragraph that distinguishes the two mechanisms as complementary. **MEDIUM-1** (`pull_requests` INSERT RLS did not actually enforce the "PR target must be source's upstream" invariant the ADR text claims — without this clause, an authenticated user could open a PR from any pattern they own against any target pattern they happened to know the UUID of) fixed by adding `AND source_pattern_id IN (SELECT id FROM public.patterns WHERE parent_pattern_id = target_pattern_id)` to the INSERT WITH CHECK clause; this also implicitly rejects internal cross-branch PRs within the same pattern, matching the ADR's "v1 routes PRs only fork → upstream" stance. **MEDIUM-2** (38.3 test budget at +15 was tight — five use cases + ViewModel needs 18–29 tests by precedent from Phase 36.3 / 37.2) fixed by bumping to +20–25, with a parallel update on the JA summary table. **MEDIUM-3** (JA summary omitted `common_ancestor_revision_id` from the column list, so an implementer reading only the JA for 38.1 would miss a required NOT NULL column + its client-side computation logic) fixed by reflowing the JA §1 schema bullet to include the column and the new fork-relationship RLS clause. **LOW-1** (fast-forward strategy description contradicted the implementation note — first paragraph defined FF as "tip-pointer move with no new revision row", second paragraph said v1 always produces a squash commit) fixed by rewording: v1 FF is "the resulting squash revision's document is byte-identical to source_tip's document — no conflicts, no target-side divergence", still produces a new revision row, with explicit note that true Git-style FF is reserved as a SQL enum value but no client path exercises it in 38.4. **LOW-2** (FK target `chart_revisions(revision_id)` not `chart_revisions(id)` deserved a comment so future readers don't "fix" it back to the PK) fixed by adding an inline comment documenting that the FK targets the standalone UNIQUE per ADR-013 §1 and matches the `chart_branches.tip_revision_id` precedent. Pre-push invariants green (`bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` — 301 keys, unchanged since this slice is doc-only). 1033 shared tests (unchanged — no code touched). **Scope cut**: PR open / close / merge / comment use cases land in 38.3 / 38.4; no migration ships in this slice. Migration 016 lands in 38.1 alongside the schema + RPC.

- **Phase 37.3**: Chart diff view (ADR-013 §5 §6 §9) — third code slice of Phase 37, the read-side culmination that turns the 37.1 history spine + 37.2 history list into a side-by-side comparison surface. Closes the no-op `onRevisionClick` callback Phase 37.2 left in NavGraph at the `composable<ChartHistory>` block. **Domain**: `ChartDiff` envelope (`base: StructuredChart?`, `target: StructuredChart`, `cellChanges: List<CellChange>`, `layerChanges: List<LayerChange>`) under `domain/model/`. `base` is nullable so the initial-commit case (no parent → "Initial commit" view per ADR §6) loads cleanly without a special enum branch. Derived `isInitialCommit` / `addedCellCount` / `modifiedCellCount` / `removedCellCount` / `hasNoChanges` properties keep the UI free of recount loops. `CellChange` sealed interface (`Added` / `Removed` / `Modified`) with `layerId` + `x` / `y` resolved through a position-keyed contract — `Modified.before.x == Modified.after.x` by construction since the diff keys cells by `(x, y)` (a cell whose position moved is one Add + one Remove, NOT a "moved" category, per ADR-013 §5). `LayerChange` sealed interface (`Added` / `Removed` / `PropertyChanged`) — `PropertyChanged.before` and `.after` carry the full pre/post layer so the renderer can derive name / visible / locked deltas at the call site without a Kotlin enum union. **Diff algorithm**: `domain/chart/ChartDiffAlgorithm.kt` pure object with `diff(base: StructuredChart?, target: StructuredChart): ChartDiff`. Implements ADR §5 verbatim: layer-id union → categorize as Added / Removed / PropertyChanged; for shared layers, cell `(x, y)` union → categorize as CellAdded / CellRemoved / CellModified. **Cells in entirely-added or entirely-removed layers are NOT enumerated in `cellChanges`** — the layer-level event implies them; this prevents an N-cell blow-up when a 100-cell layer is added (one `LayerAdded` vs 100 `CellAdded`). Polar charts diff identically since `(cell.x, cell.y) = (stitch, ring)` is the canonical address regardless of `CoordinateSystem`. Parametric symbols diff via `ChartCell` data class equality — `symbolParameters` participates in `==` so a parameter-only edit surfaces as `CellModified`. O(N + M) over total cell counts; ~10K cells per side runs well under a millisecond, no memoization needed. **Use case**: `GetChartDiffUseCase(repository: ChartRevisionRepository)` with `suspend operator fun invoke(baseRevisionId: String?, targetRevisionId: String): UseCaseResult<ChartDiff>`. `baseRevisionId` nullable for initial-commit. `targetRevisionId` required — a missing target is hard `NotFound`. **`baseRevisionId` non-null + lookup miss is also `NotFound`** (semantically distinct from `baseRevisionId == null` initial-commit which succeeds with `isInitialCommit=true`) — silently degrading would hide a sync drift between `chart_documents.revision_id` and `chart_revisions` (ADR-013 Consequences→Negative §2 reverse-failure window). Both `getRevision` calls are `try { ... } catch (e: Exception) { e.toUseCaseError() }` — explicit `Exception` catch (not `runCatching`) so `CancellationException` propagates correctly. Wired through `UseCaseModule` Koin factory. **`ChartDiffViewModel`** — StateFlow holding `ChartDiffState(diff: ChartDiff?, isLoading: Boolean, error: String?)`. Single `init { load() }` resolves the diff once via `viewModelScope.launch` (no Flow observation — diff is a one-shot snapshot of two immutable revisions; Phase 37 has no scenario where revisions mutate after creation per the immutability invariant). `ClearError` event nulls the surfaced error. Snackbar consumer matches the `ChartHistoryScreen` pattern; raw error message per the project-wide "ViewModel error-message localization" Tech Debt deferral. **Channel pivot for tap routing**: 37.2 emitted `Channel<String>` carrying just the tapped `revisionId`. 37.3 pivots to `Channel<RevisionTapTarget>` carrying `(targetRevisionId, baseRevisionId?)`. The lookup happens in `ChartHistoryViewModel.onEvent(TapRevision)` because the ViewModel owns the revision graph — looks up the tapped row in `_state.value.revisions` and emits both ids. Unknown revisionId race emits `baseRevisionId = null` rather than crashing the navigation pipeline (test coverage included). Compose `ChartHistoryScreen` `onRevisionClick: (baseRevisionId: String?, targetRevisionId: String) -> Unit` callback signature changed accordingly; iOS bridge `wrapChartHistoryRevisionTaps` typed-rebound from `Flow<String>` to `Flow<RevisionTapTarget>`. **Compose `ChartDiffScreen`** — Scaffold + diff summary chip + layer-changes banner + dual-canvas panel. `DualCanvasPanel` uses a SHARED `transformableState` writing to common `scale` / `offsetX` / `offsetY` `mutableFloatStateOf` consumed by both panes via `graphicsLayer` — synchronized pan/zoom across the two canvases, the load-bearing UX engineering ADR-013 Negative §3 flagged as the hardest 37.3 risk surface. Highlight palette is traffic-light green (added) / yellow (modified) / red (removed) at 0.4 alpha — DELIBERATELY DISTINCT from the per-segment overlay's `onSurface` / `primary` palette per ADR-013 Considered alternatives row 8 (avoiding visual-language overload). `ChartDiffCanvas` paints under-glyph highlights then symbol paths via the shared `drawSymbolPath` / `polarLayoutFor` / `drawPolarGrid` / `drawPolarCells` helpers from `SymbolDrawing.kt` + `PolarDrawing.kt` (no duplication). New private helpers `drawRectDiff` (rect renderer with grid + per-cell highlight rect under glyph) + `drawPolarDiffOverlay` (polar wedge highlights painted via `polarWedgePath`). Initial commit (`diff.base == null`) renders `label_initial_commit` in the base pane instead of an empty canvas — clear semantic signal vs an empty rendering void. `state_no_changes` empty state when both revisions are byte-identical (common when comparing a `content_hash` collision). testTags per ADR §6: `chartDiffScreen` (root landmark), `diffSummaryChip`, `baseChartCanvas`, `targetChartCanvas`, `layerChangesBanner`, `backButton`. **NavGraph**: new `@Serializable data class ChartDiff(baseRevisionId: String?, targetRevisionId: String)` route. `composable<ChartDiff>` block consumes the route. The 37.2 `composable<ChartHistory>` `onRevisionClick = { _ -> }` no-op is pivoted to `{ baseRevisionId, targetRevisionId -> navController.navigate(ChartDiff(...)) }`. **iOS mirror**: `iosApp/.../ChartDiffScreen.swift` uses `ScopedViewModel<ChartDiffViewModel, ChartDiffState>` per the established holder pattern. SwiftUI `MagnificationGesture().simultaneously(with: DragGesture())` drives shared `@State scale: CGFloat` / `lastScale` / `offset: CGSize` / `lastOffset` — synchronized pan/zoom mirror of the Compose pattern. Highlight colors hand-tuned to the same 0.4-alpha traffic-light palette via `Color(red:green:blue:).opacity(0.4)`. `DiffCanvas` struct holds a private `PathCommandCache` final class that mirrors the Compose `parsedPathCache` map (avoids re-parsing SVG paths per render). `drawSymbolPath` / `polarLayout` / `polarWedgePath` / `cellRect` inlined in the diff screen file rather than refactored out of `StructuredChartViewerScreen`'s private `ChartCanvasView` struct — refactoring the gestural canvas is out of scope for 37.3, and same scope-cut precedent as 36.4's iOS Discovery thumbnail. The inline helpers carry an explicit "refactor to a shared helper if a third consumer surfaces" comment block. iOS classification mirror `classifyCells(diff:)` matches the Compose private function signature so reading both implementations side-by-side stays straightforward. `ChartHistoryScreen.swift` accepts a `Binding<NavigationPath>` and the `revisionTaps` collect closure now appends `Route.chartDiff(baseRevisionId:targetRevisionId:)` on each emission. `AppRouter.swift` gains the `Route.chartDiff` case + Hashable conformance + destinationView mapping. `ViewModelFactory.swift` + `KoinHelper.kt` bridge gain the `chartDiffViewModel(baseRevisionId:targetRevisionId:)` accessor + `wrapChartDiffState` / typed `wrapChartHistoryRevisionTaps` rebind. `xcodegen generate` regenerated `iosApp.xcodeproj` to register `ChartDiffScreen.swift`. **i18n** — 10 new keys across all 5 sources (293 total, +10): `title_chart_diff`, `label_diff_summary` parametric (`%1$d added · %2$d modified · %3$d removed` EN; JA `追加 %1$d ・ 変更 %2$d ・ 削除 %3$d` reorders with the 「追加」prefix per natural Japanese reading), `label_layer_renamed` parametric (`%1$s → %2$s` — same shape both languages, U+2192 arrow), 6 non-parametric `label_layer_{hidden,shown,locked,unlocked,added,removed}` (the layer's current name renders as a sibling Text in the banner so the verb is the change category; this avoids a parametric `%1$s hidden` / `%1$s shown` family that would balloon translation work without UX gain), `state_no_changes`.
