Reuses `label_initial_commit` from 37.2 + `action_back` / `title_error` / `action_ok`. iOS xcstrings parametric specifiers use `%1$@` for strings + `%1$d` for ints per the SwiftUI native formatter convention (same idiom as the `label_activity_*_by` family from Phase 33.1.7). **Tests** — +16 commonTest in `GetChartDiffUseCaseTest` covering: target lookup miss → NotFound; base lookup miss → NotFound (distinct from initial-commit success); base null → initial-commit diff with every layer Added; identical revisions → hasNoChanges; cell add/remove/modify-in-place; parametric symbol parameter edit (CellModified via `ChartCell.symbolParameters` equality); cell move surfaces as add+remove (no "moved" pairing); layer added → LayerAdded with no cell enumeration; layer removed → LayerRemoved with no cell enumeration; layer renamed → LayerPropertyChanged + cells diff in place; visibility/locked toggle → LayerPropertyChanged; polar revisions diff identically with stitch/ring keying; multi-layer mixed changes all surfaced in one diff; envelope carries base + target charts for renderer reuse. Test fake `FakeRepo` only implements `getRevision`; `getHistoryForPattern` + `append` are `error("Not used by GetChartDiffUseCase")` so a future refactor that accidentally reaches them through this fake fails loudly. +2 commonTest delta in `ChartHistoryViewModelTest` (replaced 1 old "channel emits target id" test with 3 new tests covering the RevisionTapTarget envelope: null parent on initial commit, parent resolution from tapped row, unknown revisionId emits null base instead of crashing). 1018 shared tests (+18 from 1000 baseline; ADR-013 §9's +12–18 target band, hit the upper bound). Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Kover exclusion**: `ChartDiffScreenKt*` added to the Compose-UI exclusion list alongside the other screen-level Composables. `ChartDiffViewModel` deliberately NOT excluded (testable load path). `ChartDiffAlgorithm` not excluded — pure logic, fully tested. **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1018), `:shared:koverVerify`, `bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` (293 keys). iOS build via `xcodegen generate && xcodebuild -project iosApp.xcodeproj -scheme iosApp -destination 'generic/platform=iOS Simulator' -configuration Debug build` ✅ (one pre-existing `Color(red:green:blue:).opacity(0.4)` warning in non-37.3 code — `ld` warning about iOS 17.2 vs 17.0 simulator linker version is the existing CMP framework drift, unrelated). **Ktlint recurring gotcha**: my initial `Modifier.fillMaxSize().padding(4.dp)` chain in the `DualCanvasPanel`'s base + target `Box` modifiers triggered "Parameter should start on a newline" when later wrapped — `:shared:ktlintFormat` auto-fixed by splitting the chain across lines. Same recurring class as the Phase 32.2 / 33.4 / 35.1c / 36.3 / 37.1 multiline-formatting gotcha. **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-013 §9**: branch picker + restore-revision flows reserved for 37.4 (the `action_restore_revision` / `dialog_restore_revision_*` keys shipped inert in 37.2 are still inert here). Maestro E2E flow deferred — flow needs a pre-seeded chart-with-multi-revision fixture which adds ~120 LOC Maestro setup (chart create → row count edit → save → repeat) with no clear value gain over the 16 use-case tests + 3 ViewModel tap-routing tests; reopen if Phase 37.4 surfaces a real interaction-flow regression. Fork-of-fork ancestry walk in attribution UI deferred per ADR-012 §8. Cached PNG revision thumbnails for the history-list path also still deferred per ADR-013 §11 (reuse Phase 36.4 live-render `ChartThumbnail` if the diff history surfaces a perf regression — diff screen renders two full canvases so a PNG cache would save more compute here than at the history list level if it ever became a bottleneck). **Closes Phase 37 read-side**: with this slice, the entire ADR-013 §1–§6 read path — append-only history schema (37.1) → live history list (37.2) → side-by-side diff (37.3) — is end-to-end functional. Phase 37.4 wraps the branch / restore write path on top.

- **Phase 37.2**: Chart history read surface (ADR-013 §6, §9) — second code slice of Phase 37 builds the read-side UX on top of 37.1's data spine. **Use cases**: `GetChartHistoryUseCase` wraps `ChartRevisionRepository.observeHistoryForPattern` for the live ViewModel flow + a paginated suspend `invoke(patternId, limit, offset)` returning `UseCaseResult<List<ChartRevision>>` for forward-compat with 37.4's pagination needs. `GetChartRevisionUseCase` wraps `getRevision(revisionId)` returning `UseCaseResult<ChartRevision?>` — both ship together so Phase 37.3's `ChartDiffScreen` load path can `get(revisionId)` against either side of a diff without further DI churn (the doc comment on `GetChartRevisionUseCase` is explicit about this 37.3 forward-compat justification, addressing the "reserved key ships unused" concern by routing through DI today even though no caller exists in 37.2). **Koin**: both use cases registered as `factory { ... }` in `UseCaseModule`; `ChartHistoryViewModel` registered as parameterized `viewModel { params -> ChartHistoryViewModel(patternId = params.get(), getChartHistory = get()) }` in `ViewModelModule`. **i18n** — 8 new keys across all 5 sources (283 total, +8): `title_chart_history`, `state_no_chart_history`, `state_no_chart_history_body`, `label_auto_save`, `label_initial_commit`, plus the three Phase 37.4 reserved keys `action_restore_revision` / `dialog_restore_revision_title` / `dialog_restore_revision_body` that ship inert today (the long-press → "Restore as new commit" affordance is reserved for 37.4 per ADR-013 §6 — UX shape is consistent end-to-end; only the wiring lands later). The strings.xml comment block in the EN source documents this convention so future readers understand why three keys appear with no `import` site. **`ChartHistoryViewModel`** — StateFlow + `Channel<String>` for one-shot tap-to-navigate events. Channel is `BUFFERED` so taps queued before the consumer attaches still deliver (e.g. SwiftUI `.task { }` may attach a frame after view binds). `revisionTaps: Flow<String>` exposed for both Compose `LaunchedEffect` and iOS `EventFlowWrapper.collect`. `init { }` collects `getChartHistory.observe(patternId).onEach { ... }.catch { ... }.launchIn(viewModelScope)` mirroring the `ActivityFeedViewModel` pattern — `Flow.catch` operator does NOT swallow `CancellationException` (kotlinx.coroutines library guarantee), so cancellation propagates through correctly. **Compose `ChartHistoryScreen`** — Scaffold + LazyColumn (newest-first per the repo's `created_at DESC` query). `RevisionRow` headline = `commitMessage` if non-blank, else `label_initial_commit` if `parentRevisionId == null`, else `label_auto_save`. Timestamp via existing `Instant.formatFull()` ext. testTags per ADR §6: `chartHistoryScreen` (root landmark), `revisionRow_<revisionId>` (per-row), `commitMessageLabel_<revisionId>`, `revisionTimestampLabel_<revisionId>`. Snackbar surfaces transient flow errors raw per the project-wide "ViewModel error-message localization" Tech Debt deferral (matches ActivityFeedScreen). **NavGraph** — `@Serializable data class ChartHistory(patternId: String)` route + `composable<ChartHistory>` block. The `onRevisionClick` callback is wired to a no-op for 37.2 (TODO comment naming Phase 37.3 `ChartDiff` as the future routing target); the ViewModel still emits the tapped revisionId on the channel for test coverage so 37.3 swaps the no-op for `navController.navigate(ChartDiff(...))` without touching the ViewModel layer. **Entry points**: (a) `ChartViewerScreen` Compose TopAppBar gains `actions = { IconButton(MoreVert) → DropdownMenu("View history") }` with `overflowMenuButton` + `viewHistoryMenuItem` testTags; new `onHistoryClick: () -> Unit` screen prop wired through NavGraph to `navController.navigate(ChartHistory(patternId))`. New `onChartHistoryClick: (String) -> Unit` screen-level prop threaded through `PatternInfoSection`. **iOS mirror** — `iosApp/.../ChartHistoryScreen.swift` uses `ScopedViewModel<ChartHistoryViewModel, ChartHistoryState>` per the established Phase 27.1 holder pattern. `ContentUnavailableView(LocalizedStringKey("state_no_chart_history"), …, description: Text(LocalizedStringKey("state_no_chart_history_body")))` for empty state. `List(state.revisions, id: \.revisionId)` rendering `RevisionRow` with `.contentShape(Rectangle()).onTapGesture { ... }` so the entire row catches the tap. `revisionTaps` channel collected via `.task { observeRevisionTaps() } / .onDisappear { closeable.close() }` lifecycle pattern from `DiscoveryScreen.swift` — `.task { }` re-fires on every view re-appearance so the helper closes any prior subscription before creating a new one (Phase 32.2 / 36.5 iOS Closeable leak audit pattern). `revisionTapCloseable` is reset on re-appearance and closed on disappear so background/foreground cycles do not leak Closeables. **`KoinHelper.kt`** — adds `getChartHistoryViewModel(patternId)` accessor + `wrapChartHistoryState` the Compose `DropdownMenu`. accessibilityIdentifiers `overflowMenuButton` + `viewHistoryMenuItem`. **`ProjectDetailScreen.swift`** `patternInfoSection` — new `onChartHistoryTap: @escaping () -> Void` Same recurring class as the Phase 32.2 / 33.4 / 35.1c / 36.3 multiline-formatting gotchas. **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-013 §9**: no diff view yet (`ChartDiffScreen` ships in 37.3); long-press → "Restore as new commit" reserved for 37.4 (the i18n keys ship today; the gesture wiring lands later); Maestro E2E flow deferred — flow needs a pre-seeded chart-with-revisions fixture which adds ~80 LOC Maestro setup with no clear value gain over the 7 ViewModel tests; reopen if Phase 37.3 surfaces a real interaction-flow regression.

- **Phase 37.1**: Collaboration core data spine (ADR-013 §1, §2, §3, §4, §7, §8) — first code slice of Phase 37, lands the append-only history schema + repository plumbing without any UI surface. Sets up `chart_revisions` as a sibling table to `chart_documents` (preserved as the tip pointer) and `chart_branches` for the upcoming 37.4 picker. **Migration 015** (`015_chart_revisions.sql`): `chart_revisions` table with `(pattern_id, revision_id)` UNIQUE + standalone `UNIQUE (revision_id)` so `chart_branches.tip_revision_id UUID REFERENCES chart_revisions(revision_id) ON DELETE RESTRICT` is a valid FK. `author_id UUID REFERENCES profiles(id) ON DELETE SET NULL` is **nullable** per ADR-013 §1 — `NOT NULL + ON DELETE SET NULL` would be a Postgres contradiction (the SET NULL action would fail the NOT NULL constraint and account-deletion would error rather than preserve the row); INSERT-time RLS still enforces `author_id = auth.uid()`. RLS exposes `SELECT` (own + public-pattern read parity with `chart_documents`) + `INSERT` (own only); no UPDATE/DELETE policies — revisions are immutable once written, mirroring Git's append-only invariant. `chart_branches` table with `(pattern_id, branch_name)` UNIQUE + the hard FK to `chart_revisions(revision_id)` with `ON DELETE RESTRICT` (stricter than the soft mirror between `chart_documents.revision_id` and `chart_revisions.revision_id` — branches are the entry point for SwitchBranchUseCase and a dangling tip would surface as a null chart with no recovery path; ADR-013 §7). Both tables added to `supabase_realtime` publication. **SQLDelight schemas**: `ChartRevision.sq` + `ChartBranch.sq` mirror the Postgres tables with `author_id TEXT` nullable + `commit_message TEXT` nullable. Both `.sq` files pair with `5.sqm` containing the same `CREATE TABLE`s for the SQLite migration path. Queries: `getById`, `getByRevisionId`, `getHistoryForPattern` (LIMIT/OFFSET-paginated, ORDER BY `created_at DESC`), `observeHistoryForPattern`, `countForPattern`, `insert`, `upsert` (INSERT OR IGNORE on `(pattern_id, revision_id)` for idempotent Realtime backfill), `deleteByPatternId`. No `update` query — revisions are immutable. **Domain**: `ChartRevision` data class (Serializable) with the same envelope shape as `StructuredChart` minus `updatedAt` (revisions are immutable so the timestamp is single-valued). `toStructuredChart()` extension reconstructs a tip-shaped record so the existing `ChartCanvas` renderers can render a historical revision unchanged at the diff/preview call sites. `ChartBranch` data class with `DEFAULT_BRANCH_NAME = "main"` companion. **Mappers**: `ChartRevisionMapper.kt` + `ChartBranchMapper.kt` route through the document JSON envelope identical to `StructuredChartMapper`'s shape (extents + layers + craft_type + reading_convention). `String.toStorageVariant()` and `String.toCoordinateSystem()` extension functions in `StructuredChartMapper.kt` were promoted from `private` to `internal` so the new mapper can reuse them — same package, same semantics, no behavior change. **Repository surface**: `ChartRevisionRepository` interface (`getRevision`, `getHistoryForPattern` paginated, `observeHistoryForPattern` Flow, `append` immutable INSERT — no `update` or `delete`; cleanup happens transitively via `pattern_id` `ON DELETE CASCADE` in migration 015). `ChartRevisionRepositoryImpl` follows the local-first / remote-fallback / sync-or-enqueue pattern from `StructuredChartRepositoryImpl`. **`StructuredChartRepository` extension**: `create()`, `update()`, and `forkFor()` all now call a private `appendRevisionFromTip(...)` that writes a fresh `ChartRevision` mirroring the chart's drawing payload + lineage. `update()` reads `previousChart` from the local DS BEFORE the local update and threads the previous tip's `revisionId` as the new revision's `parentRevisionId` — load-bearing for chained ancestry. `create()` and `forkFor()` additionally call `ensureDefaultBranch(...)` which idempotently INSERT-OR-IGNOREs a `"main"` row in `chart_branches` pointing at the initial revision — without this, forked patterns would have a populated revision history but an empty `chart_branches` table and the Phase 37.4 branch picker would surface no branches. The new `ChartRevisionRepository` + `LocalChartBranchDataSource` ctor params are nullable with `null` defaults so existing test call-sites that construct the repo directly without seeding a revision/branch layer (e.g. `FakeStructuredChartRepository` use-case tests) continue to compile unchanged — production wiring (RepositoryModule) always passes non-null. **Sync wiring (ADR-013 §8)**: `SyncEntityType.CHART_REVISION` + `CHART_BRANCH` added to the enum. `SyncExecutor` exhaustively routes both: `CHART_REVISION` INSERT → `remote.append(...)`; UPDATE/DELETE branches `error()` with an explicit message because RLS forbids them and SyncManager never enqueues those operations (a defensive `error` surfaces an accidentally-enqueued non-INSERT at execute time rather than silently dropping the pending row). `CHART_BRANCH` INSERT/UPDATE both map to `upsert(...)` (idempotent on `(pattern_id, branch_name)`); DELETE wired for Phase 37.4 branch deletion. **Realtime**: `RealtimeSyncManager` gains a 5th channel `chart-revisions-<ownerId>` alongside projects / progress / patterns / project-segments — owner-scoped filter mirrors the per-segment-progress pattern from ADR-010 §6 (NOT public-fan-out, ADR-013 §10 — bounds Realtime cost to self-authored work and avoids the "every public-pattern revision broadcasts to N forkers" multiplier; cross-fork awareness is Phase 38's "watch upstream" subscription concern, not Phase 37's). Insert events route through `LocalChartRevisionDataSource.upsert(...)` (INSERT OR IGNORE de-dups self-authored echoes). UPDATE/DELETE/SELECT branches no-op since revisions are append-only at the RLS layer. `localChartRevision` ctor param is nullable with `null` default + a guard in `subscribe` that only opens the channel when the dependency is wired — keeps existing `RealtimeSyncManagerTest` constructions valid. **Koin DI**: `RepositoryModule` registers `LocalChartRevisionDataSource`, `LocalChartBranchDataSource`, `RemoteChartRevisionDataSource`, `RemoteChartBranchDataSource` (last two only when Supabase is configured), `ChartRevisionRepositoryImpl` as `single<ChartRevisionRepository>`. `StructuredChartRepository` factory updated to thread the new deps. `SyncModule` registers `RemoteChartRevisionSyncOperations` + `RemoteChartBranchSyncOperations` aliases, threads them through `SyncExecutor`, and threads `localChartRevision` into `RealtimeSyncManager`. **Tests (+22 commonTest)**: `ChartRevisionRepositoryImplTest` (14 tests) covers append-with-INSERT-sync, commit-message round-trip incl. null auto-saves, lineage chaining, getRevision miss + case sensitivity, getHistoryForPattern ordering / pagination / empty-pattern / patternId scoping, observeHistoryForPattern current snapshot, parametric symbol round-trip through document JSON, and the forward + reverse failure recovery paths from ADR-013 Consequences→Negative §2 (re-append on the same revisionId is idempotent at INSERT OR IGNORE; PendingSync retry on a re-fired payload is a local no-op). `StructuredChartRepositoryImplTest` gains 8 new tests against a separate `setUpWithHistory()` factory: create appends initial revision row matching tip, create bootstraps `main` branch pointing at initial revision, create enqueues both CHART_REVISION + CHART_BRANCH INSERTs alongside the tip INSERT, update appends a new revision linking parent to previous tip, update enqueues a CHART_REVISION INSERT in addition to the STRUCTURED_CHART UPDATE, forkFor appends a revision and ensures a default branch on the fork, plus a sanity case that the existing forkFor data-spine path with no revision/branch deps still creates the fork tip (regression anchor for the optional ctor param defaults). **Test fakes**: `FakeRemoteChartRevisionDataSource` (append-only mirror of the production interface) + `FakeRemoteChartBranchDataSource` added next to the existing structured-chart / project-segment fakes. **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (993 tests, +22 from 971 baseline — within ADR-013's +25–35 target range; the 3-test undershoot reflects the FakeStructuredChartRepository in domain/usecase still satisfying the unchanged interface so use-case-layer tests didn't need new cases this slice), `:shared:koverVerify`, `bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` (275 keys, unchanged — 37.1 is data layer, no i18n surface). **Ktlint recurring gotcha**: my initial `setUpWithHistory()` helper return type used `Triple<...>:` colon-spacing that ktlint's auto-format split across lines — `:shared:ktlintFormat` auto-fixed via wrapping the return-type after the function name; same recurring class as the Phase 32.2 / 33.4 / 35.1c / 36.3 multiline-formatting gotcha. **Append-then-update non-atomicity** (ADR-013 Consequences→Negative §2 — both failure directions documented): forward failure (revision INSERT succeeds, tip UPDATE fails) leaves the local history list one revision ahead of `chart_documents.revision_id` until the next sync round retries the tip UPDATE; reverse failure (remote revision INSERT fails but remote tip UPDATE somehow lands first — rare but possible if the tip UPDATE's PendingSync entry races ahead of the revision INSERT entry under heavy retry pressure) creates a temporary inconsistency window where remote `chart_documents.revision_id` points at a revision that does not yet exist in remote `chart_revisions`. There is **no FK** between `chart_documents.revision_id` and `chart_revisions.revision_id` (soft mirror per ADR-013 §4) so the tip UPDATE is not blocked at the database layer if the revision INSERT hasn't landed — this is by design (the alternative is a Supabase RPC `append_chart_revision` which couples KMP repos to Postgres-side semantics no other write path uses; deferred per ADR-013 implementer voice unless telemetry shows divergence as a user-visible issue). PendingSync coalescing handles both directions and the inconsistency window is bounded to a single sync cycle. **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-013 §11**: no UseCase wiring (`GetChartHistoryUseCase` is Phase 37.2), no UI (`ChartHistoryScreen` Phase 37.2; `ChartDiffScreen` Phase 37.3; branch picker Phase 37.4), no diff algorithm (Phase 37.3), no commit-message field on `update(chart)` signature (caller passes `null` today; commit-with-message UI in Phase 37.2's save flow). The `appendRevisionFromTip` private helper accepts a `commitMessage` parameter today — wired as null on every call site so the column round-trips correctly + Phase 37.2 can flip the message-bearing call sites in one diff without touching the persistence layer. **Forward-compat anchors for Phase 38** (PR/merge): `ChartRevision.authorId` is already provisioned and routes through INSERT-time RLS (`author_id = auth.uid()`); the `chart-revisions-<ownerId>` Realtime channel is owner-scoped by design so a Phase 38 PR that introduces multi-author commits will need an explicit "watch upstream" subscription mechanism (right shape, not implicit fan-out via channel design today). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 2 HIGH / 3 MEDIUM / 2 LOW first pass — all 7 fixed pre-commit. **HIGH-1** (`update()` TOCTOU on read-then-write — two concurrent saves on the same chart could both read the same prior tip and produce a branching parent chain): added `private val writeMutex = Mutex()` field on `StructuredChartRepositoryImpl`; `create()`, `update()`, and `forkFor()` now wrap their entire read/write triples in `writeMutex.withLock { … }`. SQLite is single-writer at the driver layer, but the read happens before the write inside the repository — an in-process race would still observe the pre-update tip on both callers without the mutex. **HIGH-2** + **LOW-2** (`ensureDefaultBranch` always enqueued a CHART_BRANCH INSERT even when the local INSERT-OR-IGNORE was a no-op, AND racing devices would both generate distinct UUIDs for the same `(pattern_id, "main")` row — the server-side `onConflict = "pattern_id,branch_name"` upsert would silently overwrite `id` on the losing device): refactored `ensureDefaultBranch` to call `localChartBranch.getByPatternIdAndName(patternId, "main")` first and short-circuit with no-op if a "main" row already exists. The local upsert + sync enqueue happen exactly once per pattern. **MEDIUM-1** (`executeChartRevision` `error("...")` on UPDATE/DELETE branches would mark the entry FAILED and trigger an indefinite retry storm on a row that can never succeed): changed both branches to `return true` silent no-op, matching `executeProgress`'s convention for unsupported operations. The doc comment now flags that the UPDATE/DELETE branches surface upstream bugs via PendingSync log inspection rather than throwing. **MEDIUM-2** (`createdAt = chart.updatedAt` could tie or out-of-order the `getHistoryForPattern` ORDER BY when a caller constructs a chart with a stale `updatedAt`): switched to `createdAt = Clock.System.now()` inside `appendRevisionFromTip` so the ordering key is always wall-clock time at append. The `chart.updatedAt` semantics is now exclusively the tip pointer's lastWrite-time, decoupled from history timestamping. **MEDIUM-3** (Realtime `chart-revisions-<ownerId>` channel handler silently dropped DELETE events, but `ON DELETE CASCADE` on `chart_revisions.pattern_id` will fire one DELETE per revision row when a pattern is deleted — local revision rows would never be cleaned up): added `FOREIGN KEY (pattern_id) REFERENCES PatternEntity(id) ON DELETE CASCADE` to both `ChartRevision.sq` + `ChartBranch.sq` + `5.sqm` so SQLite cascades locally when a pattern is deleted (matches the `Progress.sq` / `ProjectSegment.sq` precedent), AND added a `PostgresAction.Delete` branch to `handleChartRevisionAction` that calls `localChartRevision.deleteByPatternId(old.patternId)` for cross-device cleanup parity. Calling `deleteByPatternId` per-event is wasteful but idempotent — subsequent calls on the same patternId are no-ops. **LOW-1** (`RemoteChartRevisionDataSource.append` used `table.insert(...)` which would throw `RestException` 23505 on a re-enqueued duplicate, contradicting the doc comment's "successful no-op" claim): changed to `table.upsert(...) { onConflict = "revision_id"; ignoreDuplicates = true; select() }` returning `decodeSingleOrNull` and falling back to the input revision when the upsert was a no-op. Revisions are immutable once written so `ignoreDuplicates` is the semantically correct shape — never overwrite, only insert-once. Reviewer-acknowledged-out-of-scope: dependency injection for null-default optional ctor params (`appendRevisionFromTip` / `ensureDefaultBranch` no-op when their deps are null — production wiring always provides non-null; existing `SyncExecutor` uses the same `?: return true` null-guard pattern); `commitMessage: String?` always-null-today (Phase 37.2 will flip the message-bearing call sites in one diff); iOS Closeable/lifecycle (no `expect/actual` types, no `Closeable` patterns, no `CoroutineScope` leaked into iOS).

- **Phase 37.0**: ADR-013 cut for collaboration core — opens Phase 37 with the data-model + UX shape decided before any code lands. ADR sized at ~470 lines EN + JA summary (matches the ADR-012 EN+JA-summary precedent). **Key decisions resolved by the agent team**: (1) Append-only history lives in a new sibling `chart_revisions` table; `chart_documents` keeps `UNIQUE (pattern_id)` and stays as the tip pointer — every existing read path (`getByPatternId`, `observeByPatternId`, `existsByPatternId`, fork's `forkFor`, sync, Realtime channel `chart-documents-<ownerId>`) continues unchanged. The repurpose-`chart_documents`-as-append-only alternative (drop UNIQUE) was rejected because it forces every consumer to re-add a "tip" filter and emits Realtime events on every revision insert from the same user across devices. (2) Tip pointer = `chart_documents.revision_id` (no schema change to chart_documents). Write path becomes "INSERT chart_revisions row → UPDATE chart_documents tip". Append-then-update is non-atomic; PendingSync coalescing handles the network-drop window per the existing best-effort idiom. Server-side RPC for atomic append+update was rejected for MVP — couples KMP repos to Postgres-side semantics that no other write path uses; revisit only if telemetry shows tip-divergence as a user-visible issue. (3) Branch table `chart_branches(pattern_id, branch_name, tip_revision_id)` with `(pattern_id, branch_name)` UNIQUE — schema ships in 37.1 (same migration as `chart_revisions`); UI ships in 37.4. "main" auto-created on first revision. Single-tip simplification (only the checked-out branch's tip is materialized in `chart_documents`) is a deliberate scope cut — chart docs are <100KB so re-materializing on switch is sub-millisecond. (4) `commit_message TEXT NULL` column on `chart_revisions`, captured at save time. Auto-saves write null; explicit save-with-message writes the user-supplied string. Editing past commit messages is out of scope. (5) Diff algorithm is cell-level over `(layer.id, x, y)` triples; layer-property diffs (visibility, name, lock) tracked separately; layers added/removed enumerated as one `LayerAdded`/`LayerRemoved` rather than blowing up into N `CellAdded`/`CellRemoved` per cell. Position-keyed (not symbol-keyed) so a "moved" cell shows up as add+remove, not as a "moved" category — knitters reading a diff care about "what's in this position now vs before" more than "which symbols moved" (Phase 37+ can add move-detection as a post-process if telemetry shows noisy diffs after pattern reorganizations). Polar charts diff identically (`(x, y)` key is `(stitch, ring)` on polar). Parametric symbols diff via `ChartCell` data class equality — parameter edits surface as `CellModified`. Algorithm is O(N + M) over total cell counts; ~10K cells per side runs in well under a millisecond, no memoization needed. (6) UX surface = dedicated `ChartHistoryScreen` + `ChartDiffScreen` (separate screens, NOT a tab in ChartViewer). Tab-in-Viewer was rejected because it conflates "edit current state" with "browse past states" — two distinct mental models, and tab-switching loses scroll position + makes deep-linking harder. History screen reachable from ChartViewer overflow + ProjectDetail pattern-info section. Diff view uses synchronized side-by-side `ChartCanvas` rendering at half-width on tablets / stacked on phones, changed cells highlighted with traffic-light palette (green=added / yellow=modified / red=removed) — distinct from the per-segment overlay palette to avoid overloading visual language. Synchronized pan/zoom across the two diff panes is the harder UX engineering risk surface for 37.3. (7) `author_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES profiles(id) ON DELETE SET NULL` provisioned now even though Phase 37 always has `owner_id == author_id` — Phase 38 PR/merge introduces multi-author commits, and a Phase 38 migration to backfill `author_id` would be wasted work. ON DELETE SET NULL preserves history after the author account is deleted. (8) No UPDATE/DELETE policies on `chart_revisions` — revisions are immutable once written, mirroring Git's append-only history invariant. **Phase 37 sub-slice plan** (locked in as ADR §9): 37.0 (this ADR, no code) → 37.1 (`chart_revisions` + `chart_branches` schema, domain `ChartRevision`, repository, sync wiring, default-"main" auto-create on first save; +25–35 commonTest, migration 015) → 37.2 (`GetChartHistoryUseCase`, `ChartHistoryViewModel`, `ChartHistoryScreen` Compose+SwiftUI; +6–10 commonTest, 6–8 i18n keys) → 37.3 (`GetChartDiffUseCase`, `ChartDiffScreen` Compose+SwiftUI, cell-level + layer-property diff; +12–18 commonTest, 8–12 i18n keys) → 37.4 (branch picker UI, "New branch" / "Switch branch" / restore-revision flows; +10–15 commonTest, 6–8 i18n keys). Slice 37.4 is the only one that may slip out of MVP without breaking earlier slices — 37.1/37.2/37.3 form a coherent read-only history experience even if branch never ships. **Forward-compat anchors for Phase 38**: `chart_revisions.author_id` already provisioned (multi-author PR/merge); diff algorithm already cell-level (PR/merge can compute diff-of-diffs against the same shape); attribution UI already supports "Forked from <title> by <author>" deep link (Phase 36.5) which can deepen to "View source's history" using the public-pattern Realtime subscription on `chart_revisions` (RLS already in §1 of the ADR). **Explicitly NOT in MVP** (per ADR-007 "Minimal Git semantics; no CRDT in v1"): pull-request workflow (Phase 38), three-way merge (Phase 38), CRDT concurrent editing (post-v1 if ever), cherry-pick / rebase / squash / amend (out of scope indefinitely), editing past commit messages, branch protection rules, multi-author diff blame (Phase 38+), full fork-chain ancestry walk in attribution UI, server-side atomicity RPC, cached PNG revision thumbnails for the history list (reuse Phase 36.4 live-render `ChartThumbnail` at smaller scale), `commit_message` validation/max-length (UI enforces a soft 200-char limit, server accepts any TEXT). Realtime channel count grows from 4 to 5 per authenticated user (the new `chart-revisions-<ownerId>` channel is the 5th alongside projects/progress/patterns/project-segments) — bounded cost; if Phase 39 closed beta surfaces a connection-budget cap, channels coalesce then. Storage cost grows linearly with edit count (a power user with 200 edits → 200 revision rows × ~50KB each = ~10MB per pattern); retention policy not in MVP (Phase 37+ can add daily snapshots beyond N days if storage telemetry surfaces it). No test delta this slice (ADR is documentation only). Pre-push invariants unchanged (no code touched); 818 shared tests, 275 i18n keys.

- **Phase 36.5**: "Forked from" attribution UI on ProjectDetail (ADR-012 §6) — fifth and final slice of Phase 36, the closing piece of the fork-with-attribution loop that 36.1 (`parentPatternId` data spine) and 36.3 (fork orchestration write to `parentPatternId = sourcePattern.id`) provisioned. With this slice, a forker's project detail view surfaces the source pattern + author with a tap-to-view link to the source's chart viewer when the source is still public. **State extension**: `ProjectDetailState` gains `parentPattern: Pattern?` + `parentPatternAuthor: User?`. The signal that the current pattern was forked is `pattern?.parentPatternId != null` (the existing field). Three render states are derived: (a) `parentPatternId == null` → not forked, render nothing; (b) `parentPatternId != null && parentPattern == null` → source was deleted/private/lookup-failed, render plain `state_forked_from_deleted`; (c) `parentPattern != null` → render parametric `label_forked_from`, tappable when `parentPattern.visibility == PUBLIC`. **Resolution coroutine**: new `observeParentAttribution()` in `init { }` next to `loadChartImages()` / `loadProgressPhotoUrls()`. Subscribes to `patternFlow.map { it?.parentPatternId }.distinctUntilChanged()` (so a regular pattern edit that changes title/description but not `parentPatternId` does not retrigger the fetch) and `flatMapLatest { parentId -> flow { ... } }` so an in-flight resolution is cancelled when the parent id changes — load-bearing only for a hypothetical future re-link path that swaps `project.patternId` (write-once per ADR-012 §1 means the first-pass `collect` would not race today, but the structure is the correct one and matches the cancellation-safe pattern from Phase 36.3's `ForkPublicPatternUseCase`). Both `patternRepository.getById` and `userRepository.getById` failures degrade gracefully — caught with explicit `if (e is CancellationException) throw e` rethrow per the same Phase 36.3 KDoc rationale, then the catch returns null and the UI renders the deleted-source branch. **No new use case**: the existing `patternRepository.getById(parentId)` + `userRepository.getById(source.ownerId)` call pair is short enough that wrapping in a dedicated UseCase would be ceremony for one call site (matches the precedent in `SharedWithMeViewModel.kt` which calls `patternRepository.getById` + `userRepository.getByIds` directly). **`UiOverlay`** gains `parentPattern: Pattern?` + `parentPatternAuthor: User?` fields; the main `combine` block forwards them into `ProjectDetailState`. **Compose UI**: `PatternInfoSection` private composable extended with `parentPattern: Pattern?` + `parentPatternAuthor: User?` + `onParentPatternClick: (String) -> Unit` params. Renders the row right under the title row (above the structured-chart links). When `pattern.parentPatternId != null`, picks one of three branches: `state_forked_from_deleted` plain text (testTag `forkedFromDeletedLabel`), parametric `label_forked_from` plain text non-tappable when `visibility != PUBLIC` (testTag `forkedFromLabel`), or parametric `label_forked_from` clickable Text with `clickable(role = Role.Button)` for TalkBack a11y parity with the iOS `Button(action:)` mirror (testTag `forkedFromLink`). Author name resolves via `parentPatternAuthor?.displayName ?: stringResource(Res.string.label_someone)` per the Phase 33.1.7 ActivityFeed precedent. **NavGraph**: the `composable<ProjectDetail>` block plumbs `onParentPatternClick = { parentPatternId -> navController.navigate(ChartViewer(patternId = parentPatternId, projectId = null)) }` — `projectId = null` because the user is browsing someone else's pattern, so segment overlay (which is project-scoped per ADR-010 §4) does not apply. **iOS mirror**: SwiftUI `patternInfoSection` helper extended with the same params + a new `forkedFromRow(parentPattern:parentPatternAuthor:onTap:)` private helper. Three render branches mirror Compose: `Text(LocalizedStringKey("state_forked_from_deleted"))` for the deleted-source branch (auto-resolves through xcstrings per the 33.1.6 SwiftUI literal-promotion table), and for the resolved branch a `String(format: NSLocalizedString("label_forked_from", comment: ""), source.title, authorName)` parametric resolution wrapped in `Text(verbatim:)` to avoid LocalizedStringKey re-resolution of user-authored strings (same idiom as `label_activity_*_by` from Phase 33.1.7). Tappable variant is a `Button(action:)` with `.buttonStyle(.plain)`, non-tappable variant is a plain `Text`. **`Visibility.PUBLIC` Swift bridging gotcha**: the Kotlin enum case `PUBLIC` bridges to Swift as `.public_` (trailing underscore — `public` is a Swift reserved word; same trailing-underscore mapping as `PatternEditScreen.swift`'s `VisibilityOption.toVisibility() { .publicVisibility: return .public_ }`). Documented inline at `forkedFromRow`. Author-null fallback uses `parentPatternAuthor?.displayName ?? NSLocalizedString("label_someone", comment: "")`. **i18n**: 2 new keys added to all 5 sources (275 total, +2): `label_forked_from` parametric ("Forked from: %1$s by %2$s" / "%1$s（%2$s）からフォーク" — JA puts the parenthetical author after the title for natural reading; iOS xcstrings uses `%1$@` / `%2$@`) and `state_forked_from_deleted` non-parametric ("Forked from a deleted pattern" / "削除されたパターンからフォーク"). Reuses `label_someone` from Phase 33.1.7 for the null-author fallback. **Koin**: `userRepository = get()` added to `ViewModelModule`'s `ProjectDetailViewModel` factory; `UserRepository` was already a `single<UserRepository>` in `RepositoryModule` (consumed by `SharedWithMeViewModel` since Phase 5b). **Tests**: +3 commonTest in `ProjectDetailViewModelTest` (33 → 36): (a) `parent attribution resolves source pattern and author when forked` — both fields populated with full PUBLIC source + named author, (b) `parent attribution leaves parentPattern null when source was deleted` — `parentPatternId` set but no source row in repo, parentPattern stays null (deleted-source branch), (c) `parent attribution falls back gracefully when author lookup returns null` — source resolves but author missing from `userRepository`, `parentPatternAuthor` null (UI then routes through `label_someone` at the Compose layer). All 4 `createViewModel*` factory helpers updated with `userRepository = userRepository` plumbing; class-level `private val userRepository = FakeUserRepository()` field added next to the existing `patternRepository` / `authRepository` fields (kotlin.test instantiates a fresh test class instance per `@Test`, so this gives each test a clean repo just like the pre-existing pattern). Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 1 HIGH / 2 MEDIUM / 2 LOW first pass — HIGH (race in `observeParentAttribution`'s `collect` body — older fetch can clobber newer one because plain `collect` does not cancel in-flight body when a new emission arrives) and MEDIUM1 (`catch (_: Exception)` swallows `CancellationException` per the project's own Phase 36.3 KDoc anti-pattern) both fixed pre-commit by refactoring to `flatMapLatest { parentId -> flow { ... } }` with explicit `if (e is CancellationException) throw e` rethrows in both repo-call try/catches; MEDIUM2 (test isolation — class-level `FakePatternRepository` shared across `"source-pat"` ids in tests a + c) verified unfounded since kotlin.test instantiates a fresh test class per `@Test` (same as the existing `userRepository` / `authRepository` fields); LOW1 (Compose `clickable` Text missing `Role.Button` — TalkBack would announce as plain text not button) fixed pre-commit; LOW2 (no test for PRIVATE-source render branch) addressed via an explanatory comment block above the resolved-test noting the ViewModel surfaces parentPattern regardless of visibility — the gate lives at the Compose / SwiftUI layer. Second-pass review APPROVED with one new LOW (the tappable Text has no `onClickLabel` so TalkBack uses the generic "double-tap to activate" announcement instead of something like "view source pattern" — consistent with existing codebase patterns on similar tappable items, deferred). Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest` 818, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 275). **Phase 36 closure**: with this slice, the entire ADR-012 fork-with-attribution loop is end-to-end functional — Phase 36.1 added the data spine, 36.2 added chart cloning, 36.3 wired up orchestration + Snackbar feedback, 36.4 surfaced the work in Discovery via thumbnails + chartsOnly filter, and 36.5 closes the loop by making the attribution observable to the forker on their own project detail. **Scope cuts unchanged**: iOS Discovery thumbnail live-render (Phase 36.4.1 polish) + iOS toast for chart-clone failure (Phase 36.5+ polish) remain deferred per the Tech Debt Backlog; the cached PNG thumbnail column on `chart_documents` is permanently scoped to "if telemetry shows perf regression" per ADR-012 §8. Next slice opens Phase 37 (Collaboration Core — commit history, branch, diff view per ADR-007).

- **Phase 36.4**: Discovery `chartsOnly` filter + chart-preview thumbnail (ADR-012 §4 + §5) — fourth slice of Phase 36, the Discovery-surface upgrade that finally makes the 35.x editor investment visibly observable to non-author users in the public-pattern list. **Data layer**: new `data class PublicPatternsResult(patterns: List<Pattern>, patternsWithCharts: Set<String>)` envelope returned by `PublicPatternDataSource.getPublic(searchQuery, limit, chartsOnly)`. Per ADR-012 §5 the `Pattern` data class deliberately does NOT learn about chart presence — fetching chart data inline would balloon the Discovery list query JSON. Instead the data source exposes `patternsWithCharts` as a companion set populated by a single secondary `chart_documents` query against the returned id batch. The companion set is **always** populated (regardless of `chartsOnly`) so PatternCard can decide per-row whether to render the live thumbnail without re-querying. **Remote impl**: `RemotePatternDataSource.getPublic` adds an INNER JOIN via `Columns.raw("*, chart_documents!inner(pattern_id)")` when `chartsOnly = true` (server-side filter; index on `chart_documents.pattern_id` from migration 012 bounds the cost per ADR-012 §4 negative consequences); the nested `chart_documents` field on each pattern row is dropped silently by the existing `Json { ignoreUnknownKeys = true }` so the `Pattern` deserializer does not need to learn about it. Companion-set query: `chart_documents.select(Columns.raw("pattern_id")) { filter { isIn("pattern_id", patternIds) } }` decoded into a small private `@Serializable ChartDocPatternIdRow` carrier with `@SerialName("pattern_id")`. The companion-set path runs even when `chartsOnly = true` for symmetry — alternative was special-casing the call site, but the index makes the secondary query cheap regardless and the symmetry simplifies the contract (Discovery always reads `result.patternsWithCharts`). **PatternRepositoryImpl call-site**: `getByVisibility(PUBLIC)` updated to read `.patterns` from the new envelope; the companion set is unused at the repository layer (only Discovery needs it). **Use case**: `GetPublicPatternsUseCase` accepts `chartsOnly: Boolean = false` param and returns `UseCaseResult<PublicPatternsResult>` (the envelope, not the bare `List<Pattern>` per pre-36.4). **DiscoveryViewModel**: `DiscoveryState` gains `chartsOnlyFilter: Boolean` + `patternsWithCharts: Set<String>` (always populated, so the iOS Swift surface can read `state.patternsWithCharts.contains(pattern.id)` directly without bridging a Kotlin Set through ObjC). Private `FilterState` data class extended with `chartsOnlyFilter`; the `combine` block widens from 4 → 5 source flows (kotlinx.coroutines `combine` 5-arg overload). New `DiscoveryEvent.ToggleChartsOnly` `data object` event flips the flag and re-loads via the existing `load(searchQuery)` path which now reads `filterState.value.chartsOnlyFilter` and propagates to the use case. Difficulty + sort stay client-side (the `combine` block reapplies them automatically); only `searchQuery` and `chartsOnly` reach the data source. **Compose UI**: new `ChartThumbnail` composable in `shared/.../ui/chart/ChartThumbnail.kt` per ADR-012 §5 — wraps a 64dp `Canvas` with a `LaunchedEffect(patternId)` that fetches `StructuredChartRepository.getByPatternId(patternId)` (Koin-injected). Catches transient fetch exceptions and falls back to the placeholder background; the Discovery list-fetch already named which patterns have charts via `patternsWithCharts`, so a per-row fetch failure here is non-fatal. The render layer reuses the existing public top-level helpers (`drawSymbolPath` / `cellScreenRect` from `SymbolDrawing.kt`; `drawPolarGrid` / `drawPolarCells` / `polarLayoutFor` from `PolarDrawing.kt`) — keeps the diff bounded and avoids refactoring the gestural `ChartCanvas` in `ChartViewerScreen.kt`. A new private `drawRectThumbnail` helper draws the rect-grid path with no row-label gutter, no segment overlay, no parameter slot text — just grid lines + symbol glyphs (or unknown-symbol `unknownBg` rect placeholder). Polar reuses the public `drawPolarCells` directly (no thumbnail-specific stripped variant needed since polar is overlay-free in v1). `DiscoveryScreen.kt` adds the "Charts only" `FilterChip` as the leading item in the `LazyRow` between search field and difficulty chips so it stays visible without horizontal scrolling, with `chartsOnlyChip` testTag. `DiscoveryPatternCard` accepts new `hasChart: Boolean` + `onChartClick: () -> Unit` params and conditionally renders `ChartThumbnail(pattern.id, onChartClick)` as the leading column of an outer `Row` (replacing the previous single-column `Card` layout) — thumbnail tap routes through `onChartViewerClick(pattern.id)` to `ChartViewer(patternId = patternId, projectId = null)`. NavGraph's `composable<Discovery>` block plumbs the new `onChartViewerClick` callback to `navController.navigate(ChartViewer(patternId, projectId = null))`. **iOS surface**: `DiscoveryFilterSection` gains the leading `chartsOnlyChip` chip; `DiscoveryPatternRow` accepts `hasChart: Bool` + `onChartTap: () -> Void` and renders an `Image(systemName: "square.grid.3x3.fill")` button as a static "has chart" placeholder thumbnail with `chartThumbnail_<patternId>` accessibility identifier. **Live mini-render on iOS deferred to Phase 36.4.1** — mirroring it requires factoring `StructuredChartViewerScreen.ChartCanvasView` (private, gestural, ~200 LOC tightly bound with segments + transforms) out into a thumbnail-friendly variant, which is a meaningful refactor; same pattern as Phase 36.3 deferring the iOS chart-clone-failure toast to a later polish slice while keeping the data layer at platform parity. The companion-set data layer (`state.patternsWithCharts`) IS at parity, so the only iOS gap is rendering fidelity. iOS toolbar tap on a row's thumbnail navigates via `path.append(Route.chartViewer(patternId: pattern.id, projectId: nil))`. **i18n**: 2 new keys added to all 5 sources (273 total, +2): `label_filter_charts_only` ("Charts only" / "チャートのみ" — chip label) + `action_view_chart_thumbnail` ("View chart preview" / "チャートプレビューを表示" — thumbnail tap a11y label). Both `label_*` / `action_*` per the role-prefix convention. **Tests**: +2 commonTest in `GetPublicPatternsUseCaseTest` (5 → 7): `populates patternsWithCharts companion set when chartsOnly is false`, `chartsOnly true filters list to chartful patterns` — covers both the always-populated companion set and the server-side filter path. +3 commonTest in `DiscoveryViewModelTest` (10 → 13): `initial load populates patternsWithCharts companion set`, `ToggleChartsOnly flips filter and re-loads with server-side filter`, `ToggleChartsOnly twice returns to unfiltered list with companion set intact` — covers the ViewModel→state plumbing of both the toggle event and the companion-set forwarding. **`FakePublicPatternDataSource`** (test fake) gained a `markHasChart(patternId)` affordance + matching `chartsOnly` filter logic; `assertTrue` import added to test files where needed. Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Kover exclusion**: added `ChartThumbnailKt*` to the Compose-UI exclusion list alongside the other screen-level Composables. Pre-push invariants all green: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest`, `:shared:koverVerify`, `bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` (273 keys). **Ktlint recurring gotcha** (matching the Phase 32.2 / 33.4 / 35.1c / 36.3 thread): the new test method bodies routed `result.value.patterns.first().id` / `.title` chains where ktlint's `chain-method-call` rule required forced wrapping after the multiline `assertEquals(...)` constructor reformat. `:shared:ktlintFormat` auto-fixed; the diff stayed equivalent (just split each `.` chain across multiple lines). **Scope cuts unchanged**: iOS live mini-render Phase 36.4.1 polish; "Forked from" attribution UI on ProjectDetail Phase 36.5; iOS toast for chart-clone failure Phase 36.5+ polish. Cached PNG thumbnail column on `chart_documents` is permanently scoped to "if telemetry shows perf regression" per ADR-012 §8.

- **Phase 36.3**: Fork-orchestration use-case wiring (ADR-012 §3, §7) — third slice of Phase 36, the use-case layer that ties together 36.1's `parentPatternId` data spine and 36.2's `StructuredChartRepository.forkFor` repo method. Closes the in-code anchor comment that 36.1 left in `ForkPublicPatternUseCase.kt`. **Use case**: `ForkPublicPatternUseCase` gains a `StructuredChartRepository` ctor param (5 params total — Koin `factory` line in `UseCaseModule.kt` updated to `factory { ForkPublicPatternUseCase(get(), get(), get(), get(), getOrNull()) }`). The `sourcePattern.copy(...)` block now writes `parentPatternId = sourcePattern.id` — the actual write that the 36.1 spine was provisioned for. Chart clone runs **after** `patternRepository.create(forkedPattern)` and **before** `projectRepository.create(forkedProject)` per ADR-012 §3 sequence. **Best-effort semantics (ADR-012 §7)**: chart-clone failure does NOT roll back the already-created pattern + the about-to-be-created project — surfaced via two new fields on `ForkedProject`. **Cancellation safety**: manual try/catch around the `forkFor` call (NOT `runCatching`) because stdlib `runCatching` swallows `CancellationException` — a job cancellation during chart clone must propagate so the rest of the use case stops writing into a cancelled scope; mirrors the outer try/catch's CancellationException-rethrow pattern. The inner catch only catches `Exception`, so the surfaced error is guaranteed to be `Exception`-typed and `(chartCloneResult.exceptionOrNull() as Exception?)?.toUseCaseError()` is safe (in-code comment explains the type-narrowing — initially had a defensive `if (it is Exception) ... else UseCaseError.Unknown(it)` branch but the `else` was dead since the inner `catch` only catches `Exception`; code review LOW1 simplified to the cast). **`ForkedProject` envelope**: the data class lives in `ForkSharedPatternUseCase.kt` (shared between the two fork use cases since Phase 26). Gains `chartCloned: Boolean = false` and `chartCloneError: UseCaseError? = null` with safe defaults so `ForkSharedPatternUseCase`'s call site at line 110 (no chart clone there per Phase 36 scope being Discovery-only — direct sharing from Phase 4b is out of scope per ADR-012 §8) compiles unchanged via the defaults. **`forkFor` returns null when the source has no chart** — that is NOT a failure. The Boolean-mapping `Result.success(cloned != null)` distinguishes three states: (a) `Result.success(true)` cloned, (b) `Result.success(false)` source had no chart, (c) `Result.failure(e)` clone threw. **DiscoveryViewModel channel pivot**: `Channel<String>` (carrying just projectId) → `Channel<DiscoveryForkResult>` carrying a tri-state payload `(projectId, chartCloned, chartCloneFailed)`. The third field `chartCloneFailed = result.value.chartCloneError != null` exists specifically so the Snackbar can distinguish "metadata-only public pattern → no chart to clone → success path" from "chartful pattern hit transient storage failure → degraded path". Branching the Snackbar on `chartCloned` alone (the initial implementation, caught by code review MEDIUM1) would surface the failure copy on every metadata-only fork, which is a UX regression: a public pattern may legitimately never have had a chart, and telling the user "chart copy failed — try re-forking" in that case is misleading. iOS `KoinHelper.kt` bridge renamed `wrapDiscoveryForkedProjectIdFlow` → `wrapDiscoveryForkedProjectFlow`. SwiftUI `DiscoveryScreen.swift` consumer reads `result.projectId` for navigation. **Snackbar — Compose only by design**: Compose Discovery surfaces the success/failure copy via `launch { snackbarHostState.showSnackbar(...) }` (NOT awaited) before navigation; the host-launched coroutine survives the parent Composable's unmount briefly enough to render at the next destination's edge. **iOS deliberately does NOT surface a transient toast** on `chartCloneFailed=true` — SwiftUI lacks a non-blocking toast helper in this codebase, and the existing `.alert` host is blocking which would contradict ADR-012 §7 ("surfaces error without blocking navigation"). The chart-clone failure recovery path on iOS is ProjectDetail's existing "Create structured chart" CTA (same recovery path as a metadata-only public pattern). Adding an iOS toast helper is a Phase 36.5+ polish item; the data layer (chartCloneFailed flag) is correct and unit-tested today and the iOS gap is documented inline at `DiscoveryScreen.swift:142–153` with the ADR §7 citation. **i18n**: 2 new keys added to all 5 sources (271 total, +2): `message_forked_successfully` ("Forked successfully!" / "フォークしました！") + `message_forked_chart_failed` parametric-free fallback ("Forked (chart copy failed — try re-forking from project detail)" / "フォークしました（チャートのコピーに失敗しました — プロジェクト詳細から再フォークしてください）"). Both `message_*` per the Phase 33.1.6 transient-action-completion-feedback convention. **Tests**: +5 commonTest in `ForkPublicPatternUseCaseTest` (5 → 10): (a) source has chart → `chartCloned=true` + null error, (b) source no chart → `chartCloned=false` + null error (success path, NOT failure), (c) chart clone throws → pattern + project still landed + `chartCloneError` non-null, (d) `forkedPattern.parentPatternId == sourcePattern.id` (closes the 36.1 anchor), (e) project row landed in repo (separate from in-memory envelope assertion). +1 commonTest in `DiscoveryViewModelTest` (9 → 10, code review LOW2 fix): chart-clone failure path emits `chartCloned=false, chartCloneFailed=true` so the Snackbar tri-state mapping doesn't regress at the ViewModel→channel layer (separate from the use-case-layer coverage). The existing happy-path ViewModel test gained `assertFalse(forkResult.chartCloneFailed)` to anchor the no-chart success path. Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens/commas/apostrophes in backticks). **ADR-012 §3 worked-skeleton update** (code review MEDIUM2): the ADR's code block originally showed `runCatching { ... }` and `chartCloneResult.getOrNull() != null` — both subtly different from the implementation pattern (cancellation-unsafe, `Boolean` mapping logic divergent). Updated to match the actual `Result<Boolean>` + manual try/catch pattern + the new tri-state Snackbar table. JA ADR is a summary file with no code block, no JA edit needed (matches the Phase 36.1 / 36.2 ADR-edit precedent). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 0 HIGH / 2 MEDIUM / 2 LOW first pass — all 4 fixed pre-commit (MEDIUM1 tri-state `chartCloneFailed` field; MEDIUM2 ADR §3 worked-skeleton update; LOW1 dead `else` branch removed via `as Exception?` cast with explanatory comment; LOW2 net-new `DiscoveryViewModelTest` chart-clone failure regression anchor). Second-pass review APPROVED with one new LOW (inline FQNs in the new test body — promoted to top-level imports for consistency with `ChartViewerViewModelTest.kt` style). Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest`, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 271). Suite-level totals are 968 (963 baseline post-36.2 + 5 use-case + 1 ViewModel = 968 — ahead of the +5 task target because the LOW2 fix added a 6th test). **Ktlint recurring gotcha**: ktlint required two newline placements that the JVM toolchain accepted inline — `chartCloneResult` initial assignment needed line break before `.getOrDefault(...)` chain, and the `failNext = RuntimeException(...)` start in the new ViewModel test needed a multiline expression on a new line. Same class as the Phase 32.2 / 33.4 / 35.1c gotchas already documented in Tech Debt Backlog; `:shared:ktlintFormat` auto-fixes both. **Scope cuts unchanged**: Discovery `chartsOnly` filter + chart-preview thumbnail Phase 36.4; "Forked from" attribution UI on ProjectDetail Phase 36.5; iOS toast for chart-clone failure Phase 36.5+ polish.

- **Phase 36.2**: Chart-clone repository method (ADR-012 §2) — second slice of Phase 36, smallest atomic data layer that unblocks 36.3 (`ForkPublicPatternUseCase` orchestration). Pure repository surface; no schema change, no migration. **Interface**: `StructuredChartRepository.forkFor(sourcePatternId, newPatternId, newOwnerId): StructuredChart?` — KDoc spells out the envelope-id-rewrite contract (fresh `id`, `patternId`, `ownerId`, `revisionId`, `createdAt`, `updatedAt`; `parentRevisionId = source.revisionId` per ADR-012 §2 commit-rooted lineage; `contentHash` carried verbatim per ADR-008 §7 drawing-identity invariant; `schemaVersion`/`storageVariant`/`coordinateSystem`/`extents`/`layers`/`craftType`/`readingConvention` all preserved byte-for-byte). Returns null when source has no chart — caller (Phase 36.3 use case) treats this as the metadata-only fork branch per ADR-012 §3 best-effort semantics. **Impl**: leverages the existing `getByPatternId(sourcePatternId)` resolution path which already does local-then-remote fallback when online — a forker who has not yet cached the source pattern still hits a fresh copy. The clone uses `source.copy(...)` so any future fields added to `StructuredChart` are picked up automatically without touching `forkFor`. Local persistence routes through `local.insert()` (not `upsert` — the cloned `newPatternId` is brand-new from the use-case orchestration immediately above this call, so no UNIQUE collision on `pattern_id`). Sync wiring reuses `SyncEntityType.STRUCTURED_CHART + SyncOperation.INSERT`, which `SyncExecutor.executeStructuredChart` already maps to `remote.upsert(chart)` — idempotent retry, PendingSync coalescing handles offline/reconnect identically to a regular create. No new SyncEntityType. `Clock.System.now()` computed inside the impl per the ADR-012 §2 "fresh created_at / updated_at" contract (other write paths take time from the use-case layer; the ADR signature drove this divergence and matches the pattern that the time stamping is part of the fork's atomic write). **Audit per task brief — `parentRevisionId` silent-overwrite footgun**: `StructuredChart.parentRevisionId: String?` has **NO default value**, so kotlinx-serialization always emits the field on the wire regardless of `encodeDefaults`. This structurally protects against the same class of bug that Phase 36.1 fixed on `Pattern.parentPatternId` via `@EncodeDefault(NEVER)` — `Pattern` had `= null` as a backward-compat default for legacy clients (added in migration 014), `StructuredChart.parentRevisionId` has been a required field since Phase 29 so legacy clients always carried it. Audit comment added inline in `StructuredChart.kt` explicitly forbidding adding a default to keep this invariant visible. **Tests**: +8 commonTest in `StructuredChartRepositoryImplTest` (9 → 17 in this file): (a) source has no chart returns null + 0 sync calls, (b) cloned envelope mints fresh ids and rewrites `pattern_id`/`owner_id`, (c) `parentRevisionId == source.revisionId`, (d) `contentHash` preserved, (e) byte-equal document round-trip across rich layers (multi-cell, parametric `ch-space` symbol with parameters map, locked/invisible flags, multiple layers), (f) sync INSERT enqueued for cloned envelope, (g) cloned chart retrievable by `newPatternId` without disturbing source, (h) fork-of-fork chains `parentRevisionId` to immediate predecessor (ancestry walks the chain, not the original — Phase 37 collaboration concern). Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha: no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks. **Test fakes**: `FakeStructuredChartRepository` (use-case test fake) gains a `forkFor` override that mints deterministic ids (`"fork-${size}"`) so future use-case tests can assert against them — real envelope-id correctness lives in the impl test. Inline `object : StructuredChartRepository` in `ChartViewerViewModelTest.kt:138` got a `forkFor = null` stub. **Pre-push invariants all green** (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest` — `StructuredChartRepositoryImplTest` 17 tests passing, +8 from 9 baseline; `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 269 keys unchanged — 36.2 is repository-layer, no i18n surface). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 1 HIGH / 2 MEDIUM / 3 LOW first pass — all addressed pre-commit. **HIGH** asymmetry note added to the StructuredChart.kt audit comment so the next reader understands `craftType` / `readingConvention` deliberately keep their defaults (schema-v1 backward-compat anchor, symmetric round-trip under `encodeDefaults = false`) and won't misapply `@EncodeDefault(NEVER)` to them. **MEDIUMs** addressed inline (round-trip equality assumption note on test (g); FakeStructuredChartRepository timestamp-divergence comment so Phase 36.3 use-case tests don't assert on fake timestamps). LOWs were style-only or no-action. **Scope cuts**: use-case-level orchestration of `parentPatternId` (36.1's data spine) + `forkFor` (36.2's data spine) is Phase 36.3; Discovery `chartsOnly` filter + thumbnail Phase 36.4; "Forked from" attribution UI Phase 36.5.

- **Phase 36.1**: Pattern fork attribution data spine (ADR-012 §1) — first slice of Phase 36, smallest atomic data layer that unblocks 36.2 (chart-clone repo method), 36.3 (`ForkPublicPatternUseCase` extension), 36.4 (Discovery `chartsOnly` filter), and 36.5 (attribution UI). **Schema**: Supabase migration 014 (`014_pattern_attribution.sql`) adds `parent_pattern_id UUID NULL REFERENCES public.patterns(id) ON DELETE SET NULL` to `public.patterns` plus a partial index `WHERE parent_pattern_id IS NOT NULL` (forks are a minority of rows, so the partial index keeps reverse-lookup cost bounded without bloating the row-count index). `IF NOT EXISTS` on both `ADD COLUMN` and `CREATE INDEX` for idempotent re-application; ADR-012 §1's DDL block updated in lock-step. SQLDelight: `4.sqm` (`ALTER TABLE PatternEntity ADD COLUMN parent_pattern_id TEXT;` no DEFAULT — column starts NULL on existing rows) and `Pattern.sq` `CREATE TABLE` extended with the column at the END so positional binding indices for the existing 12 columns stay stable. The `update:` SQLDelight query deliberately does NOT include `parent_pattern_id` — ADR-012 §1 invariant: set once at fork time (Phase 36.3) and never changed afterwards; the existing column value is preserved across regular `update` writes by virtue of being absent from the `SET …` list. **Domain**: `Pattern` data class gains `parentPatternId: String? = null` at the end of the `data class Pattern(...)` ctor (default keeps all existing call sites compiling unchanged — verified: every `Pattern(...)` and `pattern.copy(...)` site in `shared/src/commonMain` and `shared/src/commonTest` uses named arguments, so positional shift is impossible). Annotated `@SerialName("parent_pattern_id")` for kotlinx.serialization round-trip with Supabase JSON. **`@EncodeDefault(EncodeDefault.Mode.NEVER)` on the field** (with `@OptIn(ExperimentalSerializationApi::class)` at the data class level) is the load-bearing part of this slice — without it, a regular pattern edit synced from a device whose local cache predates migration 4.sqm would serialize `"parent_pattern_id": null` and the Supabase PATCH would silently overwrite the server-side attribution back to NULL, defeating the entire ADR-012 §1 invariant. The annotation suppresses field emission only when the value equals the default null; non-null fork values still serialize correctly. Currently defensively redundant with the `Json { ignoreUnknownKeys = true }` in `SyncModule.kt:34` (which inherits the kotlinx.serialization 1.11.0 default `encodeDefaults = false` — the exact runtime that already drops null defaults), but if anyone ever flips that to `encodeDefaults = true` for another field, the annotation immediately becomes the only protection against the silent-erasure footgun. The `@EncodeDefault` is encode-only and does not affect deserialization (verified in second-pass review: both supabase-kt's internal Json instance and `SyncExecutor.kt:55-56` `decodeFromString<Pattern>` correctly populate the field when `"parent_pattern_id": "<uuid>"` is present in the wire payload). **Mappers**: `PatternMapper.toDomain()` adds the `parentPatternId = parent_pattern_id` line; `LocalPatternDataSource` plumbs `parent_pattern_id = pattern.parentPatternId` through all 3 INSERT call sites (`insert`, `upsert` insert-branch, `upsertAll` insert-branch). `update`/`upsert`-update-branch/`upsertAll`-update-branch deliberately don't touch the column — the SQLDelight `update:` query omission is the invariant guard. **`ForkPublicPatternUseCase`**: an in-code anchor comment was added above the `sourcePattern.copy(...)` block flagging that Phase 36.3 will add `parentPatternId = sourcePattern.id` here once the chart-clone path lands. The current `.copy(...)` deliberately omits the override so 36.1 ships pure data-layer plumbing without changing fork semantics — Phase 36.3 owns the actual attribution write. ADR-012 §3. **Tests**: +7 commonTest (PatternMapperTest 17 → 19, +2 cases for null + non-null `parentPatternId` on `toDomain()`; LocalPatternDataSourceTest 9 → 14, +5 cases — default-null insert, non-null insert+getById round-trip, update preserves parentPatternId across a title rename, `upsert` insert-branch round-trip, `upsertAll` insert-branch round-trip). The upsert insert-branch tests are structurally correct because `@BeforeTest setUp()` creates a fresh in-memory SQLite via `createTestDriver()` for every test — no pre-existing row at `pat-fork`, so the upsert path takes the INSERT branch genuinely. **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 1 HIGH / 2 MEDIUM / 2 LOW first pass. **HIGH** (`@EncodeDefault(NEVER)` to prevent the sync-update silent-overwrite-to-null footgun) was the load-bearing fix described above; landed pre-commit. **MEDIUM1** (in-code anchor comment on `ForkPublicPatternUseCase` for Phase 36.3 readers) landed pre-commit. **MEDIUM2** (ADR-012 §1 DDL block out-of-sync with `IF NOT EXISTS` in the actual migration file) landed pre-commit on the EN ADR; the JA ADR is a summary file pointing back to EN with no DDL block, so no JA edit needed. **LOW1** (additional upsert and upsertAll insert-branch tests) landed pre-commit, bringing the test delta to +7 from the originally-planned +5. Second-pass review APPROVED with one wording-clarity LOW on the comment block in `ForkPublicPatternUseCase` ("inherited otherwise" was ambiguous about whether transitive grandparent attribution was intentional); fixed pre-commit by rewording to make the Phase 36.1 vs 36.3 scope split explicit. Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest`, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 269 keys unchanged — 36.1 is data-layer, no i18n surface). **Scope cuts**: chart-side fork (`StructuredChartRepository.forkFor` per ADR-012 §2) is Phase 36.2; the use-case-level wiring of `parentPatternId = sourcePattern.id` and the chart-clone orchestration is Phase 36.3; Discovery `chartsOnly` filter + thumbnail are Phase 36.4; "Forked from" attribution UI on ProjectDetail is Phase 36.5. Net new commits: this is the first slice; no chart_documents or Discovery code touched. Migration 014 ships orphan-able rows by design (forks survive source deletion via SET NULL) per ADR-012 §1.

- **Phase 35.1d**: Polar tap-to-toggle for per-segment progress — closes the Phase 34 polar-deferral banner. Kotlin `ChartViewerScreen.kt` gesture handler drops `if (isPolar) return@pointerInput` + the unconditional `extents as? ChartExtents.Rect` cast, replacing both with a `when (extents) { is Rect -> resolveHit; is Polar -> resolvePolarHit }` sealed-exhaustive branch. New `resolvePolarHit(offset, sizePx, polar, visibleLayers)` helper delegates to `polarLayoutFor` (Phase 35.1b) + `GridHitTest.hitTestPolar` (Phase 35.1a) + existing `topmostLayerAt` — `cell.x = stitch`, `cell.y = ring` matches the storage convention already used by the Phase 35.1b/c overlay + glyph passes. `PolarDeferredNotice` composable removed, `isPolar` param dropped from `ChartCanvas` (dead after the banner + gesture guards + rect-overlay guard all fell). iOS `StructuredChartViewerScreen.swift` mirror: deferred-notice VStack branch dropped, `guard !isPolar` removed from both `handleTap` / `handleLongPress`, new `resolveAnyHit(location:size:)` dispatches to `resolveHit` (rect) or `resolvePolarHit` (polar). Swift `resolvePolarHit` inlines the Kotlin `hitTestPolar` algorithm because `PolarCellLayout` doesn't bridge cleanly through the Shared framework (same lock-step pattern as the 35.1b/c polar geometry): atan2 + π/2 shift, inner-hole return nil, outer-exclusive, fp-defensive `floor` + `min(max(…, 0), N-1)`. `isPolar: Bool` field dropped from `ChartCanvasView` entirely (also dropped the stale `!isPolar` guard on the rect `draw(into:)` overlay branch — dead but would have silently suppressed rect overlays if a future refactor routed polar through the rect path). Retired `message_segment_progress_polar_deferred` i18n key from all 5 sources (241 keys, down from 242) — feature shipped, banner key would be misleading bookkeeping. **Critical code-review catch**: first-pass review caught a HIGH where the `ChartViewerViewModel.tapCell` / `longPressCell` methods still contained `if (_state.value.isPolar) return` short-circuits — without removing those, the Screen-level wiring would dispatch events that got silently swallowed at the ViewModel boundary, so polar tap-to-toggle would have shipped end-to-end no-op'd despite the gesture handler looking correct. Fixed pre-commit; second-pass review APPROVED. Second-pass fix also dropped the iOS `isPolar` field entirely + added a regression comment explaining 35.1d's dispatch structure. +2 commonTest (`tapCell on polar chart toggles segment state via use case` + `longPressCell on polar chart marks segment done`) — the prior `isPolar flag … disables tap events` test inverted semantically so it was split into the pure state-check (`isPolar flag mirrors the chart coordinate system`) plus the two new regression anchors. Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest`, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 241).

- **Phase 35.1c**: Polar symbol rendering (ADR-011 §2 final piece) — paints the glyph inside every visible polar cell. `shared/src/commonMain/.../ui/chart/PolarDrawing.kt` new `DrawScope.drawPolarCells(polar, chart, hiddenLayerIds, catalog, layout, textMeasurer, parsedPathCache, symbolColor, unknownBg, unknownFg)`. For each in-range cell: inscribed-square side `min(ringThickness, 2·r_center·sin(sweep/2))` clamped to ≥1f (the `sin(sweep/2)` factor is the half-chord at r_center = innerR + (ring + 0.5)·ringThickness), bounds = axis-aligned square centered on `PolarCellLayout.cellCenter(stitch, ring)`, then `DrawScope.rotate(degrees = cellRadialUpRotation·180/π, pivot = cell center)` wraps the `drawSymbolPath(def, bounds, rotation = cell.rotation, ...)` call so the glyph's local "up" points radially outward AND the author's discrete 0/90/180/270 composes on top inside the rotated bounds. Unknown symbols: filled `unknownBg` rect + `?` glyph via `TextMeasurer`, rendered upright-along-radial by virtue of being inside the same `rotate` scope. Stroke width `max(1f, side * 0.06f)` mirrors rect's `cellSize * 0.06f`. Out-of-range cells silently skipped, mirroring `drawPolarSegmentOverlay` defensive clipping. `ChartViewerScreen.kt` Polar branch calls `drawPolarCells` AFTER `drawPolarSegmentOverlay` — overlay-under-glyph ordering per ADR-011 §2 (matches rect AC-1.2). `iosApp/.../StructuredChartViewerScreen.swift` `drawPolar` mirror: per-cell `var subcontext = context` + `translateBy(px, py)` / `rotate(by: .radians(thetaCenter))` / `translateBy(-px, -py)` rotates around the cell center, then calls existing `drawSymbolPath` / `drawUnknown` with the rotated subcontext so the same shared `SymbolRenderTransform.mapCommand` applies `cell.rotation` within the bounds. **iOS formula lock-step**: inline `thetaCenter = stitch*sweep + sweep/2` recomputes what `PolarCellLayout.cellRadialUpRotation` returns on the Kotlin side (the function is not bridged to Swift since it's a Kotlin `object` member); added a warning comment pointing at the Kotlin authority so any future formula change (e.g. Phase 35.x widthUnits > 1 arc-spanning cells) is caught in lock-step. **Scope cuts** — parametric slot text inside polar wedges NOT implemented (deferred to Phase 35.2+ alongside polar editor; rect parametric `drawParameterSlots` unchanged); polar tap-to-toggle deferred (Phase 35.2); per-ring radial spokes still outermost-only (Phase 35.x polish). No test delta (visual/rendering code, no commonTest visual-diff infra set up — geometry spine at `PolarCellLayout` already has 32 tests covering `cellCenter`/`cellRadialUpRotation` from Phase 35.1a). Code review: 0 CRITICAL / 2 HIGH / 2 MEDIUM / 2 LOW. HIGH1 fixed pre-commit (iOS lock-step comment). HIGH2 (`return@forEach` label-shadowing concern) not taken — `drawPolarSegmentOverlay` ships the identical pattern since Phase 34; changing only one sibling creates inconsistency, the current code is correct, and the reviewer's concern is latent-future not current-runtime. MEDIUMs both pre-existing patterns (iOS `max(1, ...)` type inference matches `cellSize * 0.06` line 311; `cell.x/y` type matches Phase 34 `drawPolarSegmentOverlay` usage). LOW1 fixed (KDoc note on shared `parsedPathCache` accumulator). LOW2 (`.sp` on canvas pixel value) skipped per consistency with rect renderer's Phase 31 unknown-symbol pattern. Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest` 815, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 242). 815 shared tests (unchanged).

- **Phase 35.1b**: Polar viewer rendering (ADR-011 §2) — ring grid, segment overlay, and deferred-notice wiring for round charts. `shared/src/commonMain/.../ui/chart/PolarDrawing.kt` new file with `polarLayoutFor(width, height, polar): PolarCellLayout.Layout` (inner 15% reserved so inner rings stay readable when rings is small; outer 0.47 leaves canvas margin), `DrawScope.drawPolarGrid(polar, layout, color)` (concentric ring boundaries + outermost-ring radial spokes — per-ring spokes is a Phase 35.x polish item per ADR-011 §2), `polarWedgePath(wedge, layout)` (annular-wedge `Path` tracing outer arc CW then inner arc CCW to close the region, with `-90°` shift to reconcile `PolarCellLayout`'s 12-o'clock-CW convention with Compose `Path.arcTo`'s 3-o'clock-CW-on-y-down convention), `DrawScope.drawPolarSegmentOverlay(polar, chart, hiddenLayerIds, segments, layout, doneColor, wipColor, wipStrokeWidthPx)` (done/wip wedge paint mirroring the rect AC-1.1/AC-1.2 semantics; done = filled, wip = stroke). `ChartViewerScreen.kt` Polar branch in `ChartCanvas` wires layout + grid + segment overlay + the pre-existing `PolarDeferredNotice` `message_segment_progress_polar_deferred` banner (AC-1.4). Tap-to-toggle intentionally early-returns on `isPolar` — polar gesture handling is cross-cutting with editor authoring and stays deferred to Phase 35.2+. `isPolar` flag also plumbed through the `ChartCanvas` signature. iOS `StructuredChartViewerScreen.swift` mirror: `PolarLayout` struct inlined in Swift (avoids bridging the Kotlin `PolarCellLayout.Layout` / `Wedge` data classes through the Shared framework), `polarLayout(for:canvasSize:ringsCount:)`, `polarWedgePath(stitch:ring:stitchesInRing:layout:)` (SwiftUI `Path.addArc` with `clockwise:false` for outer / `clockwise:true` for inner — under y-down screen coords this renders visually CW matching the CW-positive convention), `drawPolar(...)` replaces the prior empty polar branch. `segmentsVersion` sentinel forces Canvas re-eval on segment map mutation. ADR-011 §1 second-to-last paragraph deferral ("symbol rendering inside polar wedges is deferred to a follow-up slice") shipped with the commit. No test delta (rendering code). 815 shared tests. Commit 1e58f7d.

- **Phase 35.1a**: Polar coord transform + hit-test helpers (ADR-011 §1) — pure-Kotlin geometry spine for round charts, landed as an atomic slice before any viewer/editor wiring. `shared/src/commonMain/.../domain/chart/PolarCellLayout.kt` new object with `Layout(cx, cy, innerRadius, ringThickness)`, `Wedge(innerRadius, outerRadius, startAngle, sweepAngle)`, `wedgeFor(stitch, ring, extents, layout)`, `cellCenter(stitch, ring, extents, layout): Pair<Double, Double>`, and `cellRadialUpRotation(stitch, ring, extents): Double`. `GridHitTest.hitTestPolar(screenX, screenY, extents, layout): Cell?` per the ADR 7-step algorithm — inner-hole tap returns null (matches flat outside-grid semantics), outer-ring boundary exclusive (`radius >= innerRadius + rings*ringThickness` → null), floor+coerceIn defensive against fp boundary rounding. Angle convention: 12 o'clock = 0, clockwise positive (shift via `atan2(dy, dx) + π/2`, mod 2π normalize); stitch 0 of each ring *starts* at 12 o'clock so its wedge spans `[0, 2π/N)` and its center sits at `π/N` — a half-stitch CW offset, not centered at 12 o'clock. `cellRadialUpRotation` returns the stitch center angle in radians (compatible with Compose `rotate(deg)` / SwiftUI `.rotationEffect(.radians(rot))` since positive theta = CW rotation on screen = geometrically correct outward pointing). `cellRadialUpRotation` intentionally does NOT take `Layout` — rotation is geometry-pure, not pixel-scaled; one test asserts this contract by reading only the extents. +32 commonTest (15 PolarCellLayoutTest + 17 hitTestPolar; 847 total — up from 815). Coverage: wedge geometry at ring boundaries, 4 cardinal-clock taps against ring 1 (8 stitches), atan2 fourth-quadrant, 9 o'clock wraparound on ring 2 (12 stitches), exact inner+outer radius boundaries (inner inclusive, outer exclusive), rings=0 + zero ringThickness degeneracy guards, non-origin layout center, near-12-o-clock-from-left wraparound verifying `(rawTheta % 2π + 2π) % 2π` normalization. Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck` with one post-autoformat fix on `GridHitTest.kt` line-82 multiline chain, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest` 847, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 242). **Scope cuts explicit** — viewer polar overlay paint (ADR-011 §2) deferred to Phase 35.1b; editor polar craft (§1 + §3 mirror ops, §4 batch row-done, §5 layer ops, §6 grid resize) deferred to Phase 35.2+; symbol rendering inside polar cells deferred with the viewer wiring. The Phase 34 `message_segment_progress_polar_deferred` notice stays intact — tap-to-toggle for polar is cross-cutting with editor authoring and does not land in 35.1a. Test-name hygiene: all new backticked names follow the Phase 32 CI gotcha — no parens, commas, or apostrophes (Kotlin/Native rejects these while JVM tolerates).
